
-----title
徐州（彭城） (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1062')">1053-1062年</a>　陈师道居家。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='eb1748a24cdb479f86a83cfe363052c2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb1748a24cdb479f86a83cfe363052c2");'><span id='eb1748a24cdb479f86a83cfe363052c2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1079')">1076-1079年</a>，25-28岁</div><div id='eb1748a24cdb479f86a83cfe363052c2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　陈师道扶丧归徐州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　陈师道在徐州守制家居，四月二十一日苏轼到任，苏辙旋亦来徐，陈师道偕兄往谒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　陈师道在徐州守制家居，秦观及释道潜来徐州谒苏轼，陈师道与二人相识。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　陈师道在徐州家居，春，苏轼作黄楼，陈师道为作黄楼铭。作品：《黄楼铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1206347' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206347' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206347?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄楼铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206347")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206347_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206347'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206347'>熙宁十年，京东路安抚使臣某、转运使臣某、判官臣某稽首言：河决澶州，南倾淮泗，彭城当其冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206347_comment'></div>夹以连山，扼以吕梁，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1206347", 1206347, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>流泄</span>不时，盈溢千里，平地水深丈馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206347_comment'></div>下顾城中，井出脉发，东薄两隅，西入通洫，南坏水垣，土恶不支，百有馀日而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206347_comment'></div>守臣苏轼深惟流亡为天子忧，夙夜不怠，以劳其人，兴发戍兵，固弊应卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206347_comment'></div>外为长楗，乘高如虹，以杀其怒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206347_comment'></div>内为大堤，附城如环，以待其溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206347_comment'></div>筑二防于南门之外，以通南山，以安危疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206347_comment'></div>发仓庾，明劝禁，以惠困穷，以督盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206347_comment'></div>宣布恩泽，巡行内外，吏民向化，兴于事功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206347_comment'></div>法施四邑，诚格百神，可谓有功矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206347_comment'></div>宜有褒嘉，以劝郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206347_comment'></div>十月二日甲子奏京师，明年元丰，正月甲子，制诰谕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206347_comment'></div>臣轼惟念祗承谟训，人神同力，敢自为功，以速大戾！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206347_comment'></div>而明扬褒大，无以报称，乃作黄楼于东门，具刻明诏，以承天休而明德意，使其客陈师道又为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206347_comment'></div>臣师道伏惟吕尚、南仲内抚百姓，外平诸侯，《诗》美文武；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206347_comment'></div>尹甫、召虎南伐淮夷，北伐猃狁，功歌宣王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206347_comment'></div>君能使人以尽其才，臣能有功以报其上，古之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206347_comment'></div>臣师道又惟感而通之者道也，行而化之者德也，制法明教者政也，治人成功者事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206347_comment'></div>昔之诗人，歌其政事，则并其道德而传之，后王有作，可举而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206347_comment'></div>顾臣之愚，何与于此，诚乐君臣之尽道云，忘其不佞，冒死上《黄楼铭》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206347_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1206347'>皇治惟成，修明法度，协和阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206347_comment'></div>十有一年，天灾时行，河失其防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206347_comment'></div>齐鲁梁楚，千里四远，溃乱散亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206347_comment'></div>皇仁隐忧，临遣信臣，以惠东方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206347_comment'></div>羸老不穷，安慰抚养，发散积仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206347_comment'></div>流人如归，居人忘危，完聚靡伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206347_comment'></div>天叙地平，明圣成能，人神效祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206347_comment'></div>灵平告成，百谷丰盈，万邦乐康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206347_comment'></div>郡县祗畏，允迪圣谟，终事无荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206347_comment'></div>皇功不居，归休臣民，迩昭远扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206347_comment'></div>守臣拜手，夸大休嘉，使民不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206347_comment'></div>改作黄楼，以临泗上，述修故常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206347_comment'></div>庶臣无佞，原始念终，铭之石章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206347_comment'></div>以告成功，以扬德声，永永无疆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1206347_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　陈师道在徐州家居，家中曾有讼事，苏轼以官民避嫌，遂与陈氏兄弟停止往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　陈师道在徐州家居。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4b29c310543349dbb5fd13a3ce31ed03_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4b29c310543349dbb5fd13a3ce31ed03");'><span id='4b29c310543349dbb5fd13a3ce31ed03_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1089')">1087-1089年</a>，36-38岁</div><div id='4b29c310543349dbb5fd13a3ce31ed03' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　四月二十四日，以苏轼等荐举，除徐州州学教授，旋即赴任，馆于徐州之东禅寺。作品：《谢徐州教授启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一二。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢徐州教授启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206255")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206255'>四月二十八日，蒙恩授亳州司户参军、充徐州教授者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206255_comment'></div>误膺公举，所誉过情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206255_comment'></div>伏读训词，以荣为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206255_comment'></div>惟士之干世，如女之从人，必待礼而后行，将正身以及国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206255_comment'></div>唐虞在上，无自献之八元；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206255_comment'></div>鲁卫之间，有历聘之一老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206255_comment'></div>虽用舍之有在，乃天命之适然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206255_comment'></div>苟非其人，则为乱俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206255_comment'></div>若师道少则不敏，老而无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206255_comment'></div>窃怀匹夫不夺之心，庶几君子难进之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206255_comment'></div>是古之学，勤而无功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206255_comment'></div>自好之文，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1206255", 1206255, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>华而不实</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206255_comment'></div>然贱而多蓺，乃孔子之不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206255_comment'></div>虽穷则益坚，待文王而后作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206255_comment'></div>既所长之无取，敢有意于多求！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206255_comment'></div>岂期天幸之来，辱在荐贤之数，起于徒步，名以师儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206255_comment'></div>慄股汗颜，不胜愧畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206255_comment'></div>爝火不息，幸依日月之光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206255_comment'></div>马群既空，遂及驽骀之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206255_comment'></div>再念某羁孤百出，度越半生，方寄食于游从，期转死于沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206255_comment'></div>母子不保，更怀喜惧之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206255_comment'></div>夫妇相望，限以河山之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206255_comment'></div>惟兹五斗之禄，足为十口之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206255_comment'></div>追还妻孥，收合魂魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206255_comment'></div>扶老携幼，稍比于人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206255_comment'></div>饱食煖衣，少缓其死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206255_comment'></div>捧檄以喜，知毛义之有亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206255_comment'></div>倒道而行，顾主偃之已老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206255_comment'></div>此盖某官仁而遍爱，明以有容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206255_comment'></div>为国求才，与人同乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206255_comment'></div>顾群能之毕用，悯一夫之向隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206255_comment'></div>方施咳唾之馀，已戴丘山之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206255_comment'></div>德无以报，徒怀犬马之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206255_comment'></div>命苟乘时，愿效铅刀之用。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1206255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　作诗答学者何颉。作品：《次韵答学者四首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。此诗写作地点不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_154671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵答学者四首<span class='inlineComment2'>（黄州何颉兄弟）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154671")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_154671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154671'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154671'>津津爽气贯眉目，十五男儿万里身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154671'>笔下倒倾三峡水，胸中别作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_154671", 154671, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>一家春</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154671'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年9月9日</a>　重阳节作诗寄秦觏。作品：《九日寄秦觏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_154801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日寄秦觏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154801")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154801'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154801'>疾风回雨水明霞，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_154801", 154801, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>沙步</span>丛祠欲莫鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154801'>九日清樽欺白发，十年为客负黄花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154801'>登高怀远心如在，向老<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_154801", 154801, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>逢辰</span>意有加。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154801'>淮海少年天下士，独<span class='inlineComment2'>（各本作可）</span>能无地落乌纱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154801'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　跋杨李二公发解诗。作品：《跋杨李二公诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷九。此文郑谱未系年，据文意推测为本年九月后作，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1206300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋杨李二公诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206300")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206300'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206300'>元祐二年，始以诸科解额合进士为二十七人，而考官定者才二十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206300_comment'></div>昔熙宁中罢黜诸科以进学者，于是士兴于乡者过倍，其教化之效如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206300_comment'></div>出纳之吝，虽有司事，而非诏意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206300_comment'></div>秋九月大会群士，二公为诗以相劳之，邦人以为宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206300_comment'></div>又方请于上以复之，而皆见于诗，盖其志也，可谓贤矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206300_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　陈师道在徐州教授任。作品：《呜呼行》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷三、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_155251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>呼行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155251")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155251_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_155251_0'>① 高丽本、赵本、四库本、库注本作呜</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155251'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155251'>去年米贱家赐粟，百万官仓不馀掬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155251'>青钱随赐费追呼，昔日剜疮今补肉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155251'>今年夏旱秋水生，江淮转粟千里行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155251'>不应远水救近渴，空仓四壁雀不鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155251'>似闻为政不为费，两不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_155251", 155251, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>相伤</span><sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>两相济。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_155251_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年5月</a>　陈师道在徐州教授任，五月，郭槩自知濮州改任夔州路提点刑狱，作诗送之。作品：《送外舅郭大夫夔路提刑》<span id='poem_sentence_0_154981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154981'>百年双鬓白，万里一身浮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155259'>老稚持车车不留，归人不行行转头。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/154998?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154998'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154998'>多问黄居士，终年欠一书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154998'>因人候消息，有使报何如。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154998'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154998_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155103?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪后黄楼寄负山居士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155103")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155103'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155103'>林庐烟不起，城郭岁将穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155103'>云日明松雪，溪山进晚风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155103'>人行图画里，鸟度醉吟中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155103'>不尽山阴兴，天留忆戴公。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155103'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155103_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋处士墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（元祐三年闰十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206356")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206356'>处士讳豫，字微之，世家彭城白鹤里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206356_comment'></div>曾父惟干，谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206356_comment'></div>祖说，赠工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206356_comment'></div>父仲容，驾部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206356_comment'></div>两娶姚氏，太常少卿坦之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206356_comment'></div>治平二年，年三十以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206356_comment'></div>熙宁五年，从葬大彭乡之清东里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206356_comment'></div>始处士昆弟四人，以行蓺为名人，始大其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206356_comment'></div>其后伯仕不偶，叔、季皆早死，处士亦以疾废，而宋氏微矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206356_comment'></div>处士始学，忘寒暑寝食，博闻彊记，而疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206356_comment'></div>既瘳，屏事绝客，读老释氏书，穷名理，外死生，时以诗自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206356_comment'></div>人谓处士寿矣，而卒，天之报施非耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206356_comment'></div>既卒，子章始生，姚夫人年尚富，以礼自誓，志成其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206356_comment'></div>元祐二年，仕为邓州司户参军，而夫人卒，年四十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206356_comment'></div>于是兄子清亦既仕矣，能世其业继其声者，天之报施非耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206356_comment'></div>始处士葬，不及铭，明年闰月祔夫人之丧，乃来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206356_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1206356'>宋氏之兴，自君兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206356_comment'></div>孰厚其德，而啬其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206356_comment'></div>谓天不臧，亦既有子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206356_comment'></div>归安其居，千岁之始。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206356_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='78179da1992f4f07a1e8241e4b3e1464_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("78179da1992f4f07a1e8241e4b3e1464");'><span id='78179da1992f4f07a1e8241e4b3e1464_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1090')">1089-1090年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='78179da1992f4f07a1e8241e4b3e1464' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年7月</a>　七月，由梁焘荐举，以太学正候缺，适左司谏刘安世奏劾私往谒苏事，太学之议遂寝，但未获罪谴，仍任徐州教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1090')">1089-1090年</a>　在徐州教授任。作品：《谢人寄酒》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span>《送秦觏二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span>《和江秀才献花三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span>《次韵李节推九日登南山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span>《别负山居士》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span>《送赵教授》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span>《徐州学记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。此文郑谱未系年，然文中有“元祐四年中书舍人番阳彭公出守，使其从事告于庙而新之，又加其旧，明年学成”之语，故定于此年。）</span>《次韵春怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span>《黄梅五首》<span id='poem_sentence_0_155008_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155008'>可堪亲老须三釜，又著儒冠忍一羞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155008_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155008'>平世功名须晚节，向来旬月取封侯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155008_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155008'>北州豪杰知谁健，乞我<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_4_155008'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155008_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐州学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206333")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206333'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206333'>夫祭之有报，以反本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206333_comment'></div>是故食则祭先饭，饮则祭先酒，耕则祭先啬，桑则祭先蚕，畜则祭先牧，祭夔于乐，祭龙于社，祭弃于稷，祭皋陶于理，祭周公、孔子于学，盖自三代以来共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206333_comment'></div>然学祀周公非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206333_comment'></div>治始于伏羲，更虞、夏、商，至周而大备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206333_comment'></div>行始于伊尹，更夷、叔、柳下季，至孔子而大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206333_comment'></div>盖治成于周公，行成于孔子，故学者主焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206333_comment'></div>自唐贞观，改祀孔、颜，及元丰，继以邹、孟，其徒与后之学者从祀，而礼成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206333_comment'></div>徐故无学，天禧几年，丞相濮阳李公迪来守，改庙为学，置师弟子，请名与田，以教养之，徐人始兴于学，而仕者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206333_comment'></div>徐地东近齐、鲁，北属赵、魏，南引江、淮，西通梁、宋，四冲八达之郊，南北之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1206333", 1206333, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>亢颈</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206333_comment'></div>南守则略河南、山东，北守则瞰淮、江，故于兵家为守攻之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206333_comment'></div>其城因山阻水，四不承敌，魏太武以百万之师攻之不克，苻氏亦连年历战，力极而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206333_comment'></div>故进则可攻，退则可守，形利势便，先发后亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206333_comment'></div>是故项氏常都，临制四方，宋武常守，并护南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206333_comment'></div>晋、隋之间，实以重兵，称谓大府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206333_comment'></div>盖古用武之国，故其人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1206333", 1206333, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>悍坚</span>，恃气尚力，易为攻剽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206333_comment'></div>然质直，谨然诺，宁死不隐，故犯者虽众而易治，盖可抚而教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206333_comment'></div>熙宁几年，始置官师、广弟子员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206333_comment'></div>元祐四年，中书舍人番阳彭公出守，使其从事告于庙而新之，又加其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206333_comment'></div>明年学成，公率其属文武之士祭以告焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206333_comment'></div>于是州之学士大夫耆老子弟乐公之承上而报本也，合而为诗，以侈后观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206333_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1206333'>淮泗之间，大彭之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206333_comment'></div>伯者之馀，以武为俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206333_comment'></div>雄桀之气，用于盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206333_comment'></div>亦有仁政，莫救其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206333_comment'></div>国之有学，王教以明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206333_comment'></div>示之好恶，靡有不承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206333_comment'></div>庙学崇崇，自我两公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206333_comment'></div>皇化其东，徐方攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206333_comment'></div>桓桓三圣，七十其徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206333_comment'></div>俯偻而趋，有严其初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206333_comment'></div>有堂有庭，居有室庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206333_comment'></div>右弦左书，伐鼓于于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206333_comment'></div>成则有毁，物惟其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206333_comment'></div>前者不已，后者其忘？</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1206333_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154762' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154762")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_2_155214'>虚名自成误<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作悟，据宋注本及各本改）</span>，失得略相当。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155296'>句中有眼黄别驾，洗涤烦热生清凉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155296'>人言我语胜黄语，扶竖夜燎齐朝光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155296'>三年不见万里外，安得奋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>身置汝傍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155296'>迩来诸子复秀发，曾未几见加端章。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155296'>剩欲摧藏让头角，岂是有意群儿伤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155296'>于人无怨我何<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>憾，爱者尚众犹吾乡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155296'>平生不自解<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_155296", 155296, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>嘲诮</span>，祸来亦复非周防。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155296'>我衰气索不自振，正赖好语能恢张。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155296'>诗家小魏新有声，旧传秀句西里黄。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155296'>后生学行阙师友，临路不进空<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_155296", 155296, id='poem_note_155296_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在徐州。作品：《老柏三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_154871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>老柏三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154871")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154871'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154871'>庭柏无生意，摧残二十秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154871'>稍沾杯水润，已与岁寒谋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154871'>黄里青青出，愁边稍稍瘳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154871'>会看笙鹤下，暮雀莫深投。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154871'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154871_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154870?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154870_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154870'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154870'>英姿带枯槁，劲节阙和柔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154870_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154870'>物理有兴坏，人情成去留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154870_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154870'>稍看栖鸟集，聊待晚风秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154870_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154870'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_154870", 154870, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>解道</span>庭前柏，何曾识赵州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154870_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154870'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154870_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154869?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154869'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154869'>岁月那能记，风霜亦饱经。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154869'>槁乾仍故节，润泽出新青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154869'>色与江波共，声留静夜听。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154869'>辉辉垂重露，点点缀流萤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154869'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154869_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　夏，晁补之过徐来晤。作品：《仁寿县太君卢氏墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1206361' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206361' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206361?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仁寿县太君卢氏墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206361")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206361_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206361'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206361'>夫人兴化人，其父建隆谓黄氏后复大，谓夫人宜之，以归其子赠朝散大夫世规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206361_comment'></div>寔生五子，曰陶、隐、随、升、隩，大夫以为材，使皆就学，择师而从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206361_comment'></div>贫不惮远，夫人相之，补洗必亲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206361_comment'></div>大夫卒，家益乏，而夫人教益力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206361_comment'></div>居七年而两子仕，仲为御史、殿中、贰国子，或使或守，遂封仁寿县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206361_comment'></div>夫人既成其子，张其宗，以续其世，孙曾在前，究乐厚养，而自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206361_comment'></div>绍圣四年，司业自徐徙福，夫人于是年八十有二，闰月甲子卒于行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206361_comment'></div>随早卒，陶为宣德郎，先卒，升继卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206361_comment'></div>家世葬闽中，于时司业贬徙睦州，不克反葬，乃以某月甲子藁葬于某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206361_comment'></div>初，司业以丧过润，遇晁子补之，使问铭于陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206361_comment'></div>是夏，晁子过徐致意，师道对曰：「吾常属其私，是宜铭，又尝铭人之亲矣，其何以辞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206361_comment'></div>于是以书抵睦报命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206361_comment'></div>是秋，司业以状来，师道读之，曰：「此吾之所闻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206361_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1206361'>昔人有云，知子其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206361_comment'></div>归于大家，显有其助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206361_comment'></div>君舅君姑，既安既沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206361_comment'></div>独单无旅，弗懈弗诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206361_comment'></div>上承下御，不严以恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206361_comment'></div>自约而显，不新以故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206361_comment'></div>有费无妄，斥靡而素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206361_comment'></div>申之于家，不戒而度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206361_comment'></div>周而不积，有求必裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206361_comment'></div>人以为德，不色而惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206361_comment'></div>实实祗祗，不铭而著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206361_comment'></div>何以铭之，孝子之虑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1206361_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155224' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155224?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和黄预感秋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154779'>骥騄同群鸿雁行，登临端为作重阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154779'>南台二谢风流绝，准拟归来古锦囊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154779'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154779_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>柏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154958")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154958'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154958'>用直宁论世，名成不待官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154958'>低枝缘我有，偃盖到谁看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154958_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154772?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢端砚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154772")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154772'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154772'>王家旧物群偷后，石出蛮溪百丈深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154772'>挥翰吾非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_154772", 154772, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>玉堂手</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_154772", 154772, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>断金</span>君有古人心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154772'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154772_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>捕狼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155037")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155037'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155037'>一狼将四子，二岭走千羊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155037'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_155037", 155037, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>意得</span>无前敌，时乖阙后防。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155037'>宁知射生手，已发弩机张。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155037'>会使乌鸢饱，空令豺虎伤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155037_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155037'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年11月5日</a>　为曹州披云楼作记。作品：《披云楼记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一五。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>披云楼记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年11月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206339")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206339'>曹，故周之成，国亡而为陶，今定陶之故城是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206339_comment'></div>陶之西南有丘焉，《禹贡》所谓陶丘，《墨子》、《竹书纪年》所谓釜丘，《图记》所谓南左山，而州人所谓南鲁太师之墓者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206339_comment'></div>汉哀帝由定陶王而为天子，尊其父恭王为皇帝，置寝庙如祖宗，周丘而城，以为陵邑，今州治是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206339_comment'></div>州之北数里而近，两丘相属，六国魏王之墓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206339_comment'></div>有冈自东北屈而西南，隐如伏龙，魏之所以葬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206339_comment'></div>择地而葬尚矣，而曰魏隧王墓者，以其始隧而葬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206339_comment'></div>其后名州曰左城，墓曰左山，冈曰左冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206339_comment'></div>记曰，左山其下多左姓，故名，然莫得而考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206339_comment'></div>余谓《尔雅》「丘再成为陶」，釜者，负也，犹陶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206339_comment'></div>而皇甫谧云舜陶河滨而名，郭璞又云在定陶城中者，皆误矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206339_comment'></div>然则州之所治，犹曹国之旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206339_comment'></div>朱公谓陶天下之中，诸侯四通，货所交易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206339_comment'></div>班氏亦谓「尧作成阳，舜渔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1206339", 1206339, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>雷泽</span>，汤居亳，故其民有先王之遗风，重厚多君子，好稼穑，恶衣服，以致畜藏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206339_comment'></div>秦汉去今未久，而侧僻荒虚，商旅不出其涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206339_comment'></div>承唐之乱，田里壮少弃本业，酒食歌舞，驰狗马，饰冠屦，彊悍喜攻劫，佩刀引彊，指人之藏以为费，至杀吏士，冒城郭，皆与古异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206339_comment'></div>世亦多变矣，故常选用武吏，重法厚赏，击伐斩杀，狱市无虚日，号曹、濮为盗区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206339_comment'></div>吏常日夜讯掠證验，省文书，出购募，调兵选将，期会赴告，不得休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206339_comment'></div>故郊无台池苑囿，而府无闲馆，宾不劳赠，吏无燕赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206339_comment'></div>号为辅州大府而威重不称，岂上所崇极而下所观听者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206339_comment'></div>曹近京师，皇化所先，承平百年，风俗移易，金鼓不作，狱市屡空，吏始于其间兴筑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1206339", 1206339, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>除饰</span>，以待四方之宾与闾巷之士，而来者继焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206339_comment'></div>堂馆相望，如古诸侯居，而连檐曲室，坐者挥汗，每盛夏常闭阁谢客，于礼犹有阙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206339_comment'></div>朝请大夫郭侯之为是州，不忍盗贼其民，必以仁恕，而人益劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206339_comment'></div>振其纲目，百职具举，而府益无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206339_comment'></div>又连岁大穰，家有藏积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206339_comment'></div>其明年之春，始因其旧，广而新之，为披云之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206339_comment'></div>其地之宜与登望之乐、栋宇之制，为一州之胜，而其费盖不及民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206339_comment'></div>夫人不可以久劳，亦不可以久逸，逸者所以待劳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206339_comment'></div>劳逸相济，然后身安而事治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206339_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「仲夏之月，可以居高明，可以远<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1206339", 1206339, "Clauses/122/Comments/1")'>瞩望</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206339_comment'></div>昔吕不韦与其客记其所闻，以为《月纪》，则居高瞩远乃先王之政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206339_comment'></div>而世之吏道，致期会、程文书以为治，盖亦知其一焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206339_comment'></div>台池苑囿，燕射田渔，虽非政之所先，亦非其所不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206339_comment'></div>今夫失其先后之序，与不勤其事而受其养者，则有愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206339_comment'></div>虽然，吏之所以能有此者，岂非世之承平、岁之丰穰而政之暇豫也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206339_comment'></div>则居其职者可不知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206339_comment'></div>余常从侯而登，极目四顾，则昔之范蠡、慎到、穰侯、宁武子，与夫汉、魏之墓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206339_comment'></div>其人非万乘之君则其相也，其功誉、富贵、文学、辩议，皆惊世而绝俗，而今日之风霜荆棘，狐貉之与穴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206339_comment'></div>河、济之间，禹之所治，声烈赫然，而通川广泽皆失其故处，使人悲伤忼慨而兴起，盖可采而赋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206339_comment'></div>顾吾老矣，力不足以及此，而为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206339_comment'></div>绍圣四年十一月五日，彭城陈师道记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206339_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1206339'>陶：库本、备要本改作「邑」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1206339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1206339'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_39_1206339_0'>⑴ 《后山居士文集》卷一五。又见《曹南文献录》卷七五，乾隆《曹州府志》卷四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1206339_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_155229'>车马竞清夜，人物秀三楚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155229'>登临得免俗，兹楼岂时睹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155229'>同来两稚子，冠者亦四五。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155229'>落落俱可人，颇亦厌歌鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155229'>山月出未高，潜鳞动寒浦<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋注本及各本作渚）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155229'>樯灯接疏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>星，夺目<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋注本作日）</span>粲不数。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155229'>魏侯转物手，百好趋就叙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155229'>得句未肯吐，秀气出眉宇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155229'>水净纳行影，山空答脩语。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155229'>夜气稍侵肌，鸟骇去其侣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155229'>清游岂有极，喜事戒多取。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155229'>投静未免喧，于今岂非古。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155229'>永怀寂寞人，南北忘在所。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155229'>横岭限鱼鸟，作书欲谁与。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155229'>情生文自哀，意动足复伫。<div id='poem_sentence_14_155229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_155229'>凭槛共一默，望舒已侵午。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154904'>彭黄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>争地胜，汴泗迫人清<span id='poem_title_154956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155158_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155158'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155158'>千<sup id='poem_sentence_4_155158'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155158'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_155158_0'>⑴ id='poem_note_155158_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1206342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观音院修满净佛殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206342")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206342'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206342'>物有盛衰，人有向背，向盛背衰，人则逐物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206342_comment'></div>虽然，向则盛，背则衰，物亦有待于人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206342_comment'></div>吾州之南山太平兴国寺，山之南北凡十有七院，其东南隅别为胜果禅院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206342_comment'></div>始时寺之卧佛、罗汉、观音为盛，金谷之施，门无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206342_comment'></div>其后胜果兴而三家替矣，故像毁不饰，室毁不补，革金不鸣而突不烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206342_comment'></div>使人一视而等施，则盛衰不极而事毕举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206342_comment'></div>虽然，人所避就，物所丰悴，岂智力所能哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206342_comment'></div>元祐八年，比丘某始合众施，既新其殿，又载于石，使人请者累至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206342_comment'></div>余学于释氏，愿自效，使不请，且彊与之，况其请之勤耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206342_comment'></div>夫始之非难而述之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206342_comment'></div>积土为址，伐山出木，历日费财，世以为能而竞焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206342_comment'></div>易故而新，就下而高，事半功倍，谓因人成事而不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206342_comment'></div>惟然，故天下之事莫不皆然，岂特浮屠氏之役乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206342_comment'></div>故其说以起废为胜福，则彼固知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206342_comment'></div>院故有阁，当诸山之冲，属两洪之声，余从居者登而乐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206342_comment'></div>已而少者壮，壮者老，老者逝矣，而前者之乐又为今之悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206342_comment'></div>身既与物同其盛衰，心亦与时而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1206342", 1206342, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>迁谢</span>，则其所异者何乎，览者其自知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206342_comment'></div>淳化初，知制诰孙何以布衣来，于时曹武忠王得罪右府，以节来守，门不纳谒，而一府无过之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206342_comment'></div>院之楞严讲师惠泉召而致馆，且为治行，明年而登上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206342_comment'></div>其次路振来贰使事，而属之，且曰：「急穷而忘报，交素而远名，其僧之英乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206342_comment'></div>路未以为然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206342_comment'></div>泉意其然，去，游吴，遂不还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206342_comment'></div>路至之明日，过则亡矣，于是赋其堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206342_comment'></div>则其所兴坏，盖可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206342_comment'></div>元符元年九月己酉，东里陈师道撰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1206342_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>魏府君墓表<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣五年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年9月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206365")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206365'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206365'>君讳宗讷，字景仁，彭城安德里人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206365_comment'></div>治平几年，东人饥，天子出使振业之，募民出粟而赐以官，君于是为州助教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206365_comment'></div>其先累富，父齐，为洋州司理参军，娶胡氏，有五男子，君以季少任事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206365_comment'></div>矜恤内外，敬士而亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206365_comment'></div>缓急扣门，不以事辞，有报者未尝不辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206365_comment'></div>凡贷而后，则倍期而不倍息，或损之，曰：「人一而吾二尔，何损」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206365_comment'></div>凡质不问当否，惟所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206365_comment'></div>有来以箧，使自验而不发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206365_comment'></div>或疑焉，曰：「虽妄何惮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206365_comment'></div>且一失不复，人必不为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206365_comment'></div>及疾，属其子于母兄以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206365_comment'></div>度不可偿与偿而后者，皆焚其券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206365_comment'></div>后其兄病，胡夫人复行之，人谈之至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206365_comment'></div>君以熙宁三年八月甲子卒，年三十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206365_comment'></div>娶高氏，一男四女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206365_comment'></div>绍圣五年七月甲子，其子涤谋于其宗，自大父而下与君凡几柩，别葬于大彭乡之新城村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206365_comment'></div>涤举进士，方质谨厚，不谈人之短，有谈者弗应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206365_comment'></div>至巨恶人所唾骂，一叹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206365_comment'></div>家虽贫，不苟受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206365_comment'></div>将葬，宗不共其费，或问之，曰：「葬，吾责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206365_comment'></div>使不同，吾且专之，而况有助乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206365_comment'></div>余由是与之游，始葬，欲余铭而不敢请，既闻而哀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206365_comment'></div>昔阮思旷有好车，人欲借以葬，而难之，思旷曰：「车而使人惮借，何以为也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206365_comment'></div>遂焚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206365_comment'></div>思旷之车，与人共之，犹以为难，则余之色辞拒者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206365_comment'></div>于是申以叙之，使陈诸墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206365_comment'></div>古者葬以死，祭以生，谓鬼有知而尸无知也，故不封而庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206365_comment'></div>后之人薄祭而厚葬，既封植之而又识之，既掩诸幽而又揭于道，既守之子孙而又以累人，其为不朽极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206365_comment'></div>虽然，韩退之为铭文数十，去今几时，穹石伟画，顾无存者，而其人之事功，烨烨在人心目，如今日事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206365_comment'></div>是以知金石之不足恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206365_comment'></div>今魏氏欲显其亲而必余之述，岂不悖哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1206365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白鹤观记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206341")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206341'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206341'>徐山下泉，州治之南有平泉焉，深明洁甘，旱潦自如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206341_comment'></div>泉之上有老氏之宫，其地为彭城之西乡，皆曰白鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206341_comment'></div>说者曰，泉有鹤下焉，故名，观、乡又因泉而名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206341_comment'></div>观有记曰，唐高宗遗旨所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206341_comment'></div>余读杜光庭《灵验记》，曰天皇东封，鹤集其坛，使诸州为老氏筑宫，号以白鹤，与石文合，而说为妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206341_comment'></div>其泉与乡，盖因观而名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206341_comment'></div>庆历几年，筑州之南郭，吏从其学者求而不得，乃曲其处以限焉，泉与观始异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206341_comment'></div>嘉祐中，农者赵贞病且死，梦御鹤适野，视下如江湖，杰木行列，蛇厉守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206341_comment'></div>既度，探东山而下，乃泗上定云山也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206341_comment'></div>寤而愈，以为老氏之祥，尽其有以报焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206341_comment'></div>道士刘归真与其徒李道亨又协众而继之以成，欲载之石而属余，凡数岁十馀请而不已，则其可已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206341_comment'></div>夫老释氏之教并行于世而有衰盛，世遂以为优劣，又谓教有利有不利，皆非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206341_comment'></div>夫二氏离行而合委，其所异者，因于俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206341_comment'></div>至其隆替则系于世，世之好恶则系其习，岂今之人于老氏未夙习乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206341_comment'></div>昔庄生子休谓诸子关、老、墨、惠与己之道同出于六经，而老、庄各自为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206341_comment'></div>盖子休学于田生子方，子方学于端木生子贡，而列御寇、庚桑楚皆寓言无实，后之学者因而成书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206341_comment'></div>至汉，两刘校中书为《七略》，其叙方伎有神仙，诸子有道家，而老、庄并焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206341_comment'></div>天神地示，三灵百神，又皆出于礼官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206341_comment'></div>而今之为道者合而有之，益以符咒法箓，捕使鬼物，皆老氏所不道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206341_comment'></div>然其祈报祸祥，驱禳回起，昭昭不诬，而非余所能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206341_comment'></div>盖自聃、休而后，士不明于理而术益工，此其所以不振也耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206341_comment'></div>而刘、李二士独能有成，岂不良哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206341_comment'></div>虽然，余有私焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206341_comment'></div>刘行数千里，授天师之箓于龙虎山，而未及行，壮犹有待也，今老矣，盍辍其已能，而勤其未能乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206341_comment'></div>李方壮，可任以事而嗣其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206341_comment'></div>如是，其有不兴者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206341_comment'></div>元符元年九月甲寅，东里陈师道撰<span class='inlineComment2'>（《后山居士文集》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206341_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1206341'>可：原无，据库本及备要本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1206341_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日不出魏衍见过</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154799")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154799'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154799'>九日登临迫闭藏，老怀无恨自凄凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154799'>山头落帽风流绝，壁面称诗语笑香<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：南山有二谢诗石。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154799'>冲雨肯来寻此老，拂床聊待熟黄粱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154799'>独无樽酒为君<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>寿，正使秋花未肯黄<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：是日无菊。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154799'></div><div id='poem_note_154799_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_155267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送魏衍移沛<span class='inlineComment2'>（二字原缺，据宋注本及各本补）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155267")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155267'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155267'>积雨断行路，重江未安流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155267'>胡为冒<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>艰险，迫此米帛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>谋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155267'>岁晏风作横，未宽为子忧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155267'>卒然托异县，所得如所求。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155267'>主人如古人，待士礼亦优。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155267'>人情乐新知，岂不怀旧丘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155267'>我贫无四壁，爱尔胡能留。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155267'>子也尚不容，吾代诸公羞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155267'>勿云百里远，已作千山愁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155267'>念子舍我去，谁复从我游。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155267'>诸石吾未识，因子卜可不。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155267'>能此已可尚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，终焉致绸缪。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 原作习，据宋注本及各本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_155267_0'>⑵ 宋注本及各本作帛米</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_155267_0'>⑶ 宋注本、高丽本、库注本校：一作喜</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155267_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_155004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送河间吕令<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, id='poem_title_155004_0'>① 宋注本、高丽本、库注本作送河间令，题下引原注：子固甥</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155004'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155004'>今日中牟令，当年太守孙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155004'>独能怜此老，肯避席为门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155004'>寒日风涛壮，边城簿领繁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155004'>平生子曾子，白首得重论。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155004'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155004_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_515687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_515687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/515687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵何子温祈晴二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_515687")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_515687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_515687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_515687'>夜半风回雨脚收，万家和气与云浮<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋注本及各本作游）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_515687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_515687'>萧条寒巷荒三径，突兀晴空耸二楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_515687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_515687'>胜日登临轻一醉，下乡昏垫肯同忧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_515687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_515687'>江空峡响鱼龙落，尽放青青极目秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_515687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154965'>未免困河鱼，宁如喘吴牛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154965'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154965_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154964?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_154964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154964'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154964'>小雨断复续，回斜落晚风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154964'>寒心生蟋蟀，秋色傍梧桐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154964'>草与遥山碧，花欺晚照红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154964'>口须谈世事，目已失飞鸿<span class='inlineComment2'>（末二句与《寄寇荆山》同）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_154963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154963'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154963'>山断开平野，河回杀急流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154963'>登临须向夕，风雨更宜秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154963'>急急后飞雁，翩翩不下鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154963'>晚舟犹小待，暮雀已深投。<div class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_154962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154962'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154962'>梨埒当千户，渔防拥万头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154962'>宁须一网尽，不为百人留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154962'>密雨点急水，惊风擘系舟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154962'>百年供转徙，因病得夷犹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154962'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154962_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155262?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_155262'>平生夫铁脚，道价喧宇宙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155262'>望礼东南云，吾今独何后。<div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_155262", 155262, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>空生</span>瘦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155262'>今年退后<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作复）</span>禅，袖手不肯又。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155262'>真成菩萨魔，未免化城咎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155262'>白月悬清光，大钟得辞扣。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155262'>知止一何勇，随缘岂无复。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155262'>丰台两禅子，三请期一觏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155262'>翩然挈瓶盂，百里往相就。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155262'>古寺风雨馀，触目初邂逅。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155262'>夙昔有静缘，欢然宛如旧。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155262'>教我早自异，业成谁得救。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155262'>世故已备尝，踌躇复何候。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155262'>钻火勿停手，时来自渠透。<div id='poem_sentence_14_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_155262'>慇勤礼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_155262", 155262, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>白足</span>，吾为太山溜。<div id='poem_sentence_15_155262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_155262'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_155262_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠赵奉议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_155312'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155312'>为惠不必广，但问与者谁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155312'>受施何用多，名义以为资。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155312'>平生师友间，四海参寥师。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155312'>一穷无四壁，百代有千诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155312'>再逐越淮江，三年鲁中归。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155312'>初无赞公色，不异净名衣。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155312'>才如得风鹢，已复触藩羝。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155312'>路贫谁肯怜，语妙君所知。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155312'>我往<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_155312", 155312, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>立谈</span>间，欻若白受缁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155312'>乃知仁者听，不待辛苦词。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155312'>赵侯名教士，劲气喷长蜺。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155312'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_155312", 155312, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>论吐</span>天下公，而合吾所私。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155312'>明窗弄文墨，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_155312", 155312, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>妍语</span>含英姿。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155312'>要与识者论，且避群儿痴。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155312'>旧好无新功，终年此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_155312", 155312, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>交绥</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_155312'>未须坚百战，当即建<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_155312", 155312, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>降旗</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_155312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_155312'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_155312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　冬，参寥来访。作品：《送参寥序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1206289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送参寥序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206289")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206289'>妙总师参寥，大觉老之嗣，眉山公之客，而少游氏之友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206289_comment'></div>释门之表，士林之秀，而诗苑之英也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206289_comment'></div>游卿大夫之门，名于四海三十年馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206289_comment'></div>其议古今张弛，人之情貌肖否，言之从违，诗之精粗，若水赴壑，阪走丸，倒囊出物，鸷鸟举而风迫之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206289_comment'></div>若升高视下，爬痒而鉴貌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206289_comment'></div>元符之冬，去鲁还吴，道徐而来见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206289_comment'></div>余与之别馀二十年，复见于此，爱其诗，读不舍手，属其谈，挽不听去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206289_comment'></div>夜相语，及唐诗僧，参寥子曰：「贯休、齐己，世薄其语，然以旷荡逸群之气，高世之志，天下之誉，王侯将相之奉，而为石霜老师之役，终其身不去，此岂用意于诗者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206289_comment'></div>工拙不足病也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206289_comment'></div>由是而知余之所贵，乃其弃馀，所谓浅为丈夫者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206289_comment'></div>于其行，叙以谢之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206289_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在徐州家居。作品：《元日雪二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《次韵黄生》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《答黄生》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷三、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《雪后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_154814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元日雪二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_154814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154814'>窘兔走留迹，饥乌鸣乞怜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154814'>遥忻炎海上，还复得新年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154814'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154814_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154866?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_154866'>入竹投窗夜有声，似违残腊作初正。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154866'>三更爽气侵危坐，万里回风逼发生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154866'>呵笔小吟撩我老，闭门高卧见君情。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154866'>只今剩作惊人句，颇觉吟边意未平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154866'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154866_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155294?labeling=true' inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>阍，稚子往问鹿骇奔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155294'>黄生学诗用力新，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_155294", 155294, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>急手</span>疾口如翻盆<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作盆翻，据宋注本及各本乙）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155294'>冲风踏冻送七言，要令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_155294", 155294, id='poem_sentence_4_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155294'>迩来<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_155294", 155294, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>结字</span>稳且匀，岂不见我参寥君。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155294'>嗟吾老矣心尚存，后来得子空马群。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155294'>径须赤手缚麒麟，四大海水一口吞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155294'>丈夫意气抗浮云，道逢其人两手分，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_155294", 155294, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>妒妇</span>拊膺王右军。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155294'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_155294_0'>⑴ 宋注本及各本作叫</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155294_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_155102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155102")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155102'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155102'>送往开新雪又晴，故留腊白待春青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155102'>稍回杉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>色伸梅怨，并得朝看与夜听。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155102'>已觉庭泥生鸟迹，遽修田事带朝星。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155102'>暮年功力归持律，不是骚人故独醒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155102'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155102'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_155102_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本、库注本、张本作松</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155102_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在徐州家居，常作小词自娱，得风眩疾。作品：《与鲁直书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一0。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在徐州家居。作品：《法轮院主塔铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。）</span>《送张蕲县》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《送何子温移亳州三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《送詹司业》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《西郊二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《寄亳州何郎中二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《寄答泰州曾侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《送提刑李学士移使东路》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《和郑户部宝集丈室二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《隐者郊居》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《览胜亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《何太冲挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《送大兄兼寄赵团练》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《寄襄州程大夫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《送检法赵奉议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《送建州郑户部》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span>《送张秀才》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1206366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206366?labeling=true' target='_blank'>法轮院主塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206366")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206366'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206366'>宗本，苗姓，宿之虹人，连丧两亲，顾不及报，乃去家为道，居徐之法轮院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206366_comment'></div>庆历五年，试所诵读，为比丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206366_comment'></div>明年具戒，遂主院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206366_comment'></div>元祐元年，既老而传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206366_comment'></div>四年十一月晦寝疾而逝，岁七十一，臈四十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206366_comment'></div>元符二年二月甲子，其徒法懿、法珍、法惠、法如、法坚，用天竺法葬于某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206366_comment'></div>徐故尚法，而宗相集，鼓相闻，讲席相因，学者四来，于东方为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206366_comment'></div>而顿师禅子所不至，至则无所于馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206366_comment'></div>公始除舍修供，以待其来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206366_comment'></div>数请师说性教，而时至缘会，野俗先变，向于禅矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206366_comment'></div>其起信广道，公有与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206366_comment'></div>余与公游相好，于其葬，铭以送之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206366_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1206366'>圣有去来，维缘与时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206366_comment'></div>法无高下，悟则同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206366_comment'></div>人而有争，弃理用情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206366_comment'></div>知者不言，道则自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206366_comment'></div>孔李二氏，与释而三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206366_comment'></div>一人之传，或说或参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206366_comment'></div>人有利否，教则多门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206366_comment'></div>何以二之，白日青天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206366_comment'></div>时移俗变，昔法今禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206366_comment'></div>孰为予夺，同业而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206366_comment'></div>因则然矣，缘则何其。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206366_comment'></div>有风有自，尔公预之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1206366_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张蕲县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154996'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154996'>接禄才馀岁，为邦近故园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154996'>案图三万户，镇静五千言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154996'>雪尽春泥滑，风生沙水昏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154996'>犹须放琴客，坐席稍能温。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154987'>画地数佳政，丛谈何处村<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：尝请湖、越而得亳。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155023'>学舍论交二十年，白头相对固依然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155023_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155023'>才难孰为吾君惜，果满宁容我辈先。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155070'>已度城阴先得句，不应从俗未忘荤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155070'>松篁有节元宜晚，桃李无蹊只自薰。<div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155286'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155286'>张生服石为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_155286", 155286, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>石奴</span>，下潦上乾如渴乌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155286'>一朝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_155286", 155286, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>偾蹶</span>须人扶，伏毒未动风出虚。<div
