id='poem_sentence_3_155286'>自笑未竟人复吁，以身济欲未必愚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155286'>欲久而速反所图，嗟哉伟然二大夫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155286'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_155286_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206294?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寇参军集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206294")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206294'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206294'>大父盐铁府君、外大父颍公与文忠蔡公好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206294_comment'></div>太常少卿寇君，蔡之出也，游二大父之间而辈先君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206294_comment'></div>两君卒，二氏之子弟居同邑，学同文，情同好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206294_comment'></div>寇氏之伯曰元老，喜事而多能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206294_comment'></div>张、李氏之墨，吴、唐、蜀、闽、两越之纸，端溪、歙穴之研，鼠须栗尾、狌毫兔颖之笔，所谓文房四物，山藏海蓄，极天下之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206294_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1206294", 1206294, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>倾家破产</span>，急士之穷，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1206294", 1206294, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>轻身下气</span>而交名胜，士多归之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206294_comment'></div>其季曰元弼，一无所好，顾嗜酒与诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206294_comment'></div>方其展纸濡笔，立下疾行，倏忽数十百韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206294_comment'></div>衣冠在傍，合手起色，骇叹不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206294_comment'></div>然成辄弃去，不复爱惜，非如世之诗生窭士，牵课临仿，吻颊鸣悲，岁锻月鍊者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206294_comment'></div>昔魏晋之士，当嫌疑之际，能慕名著节，而身在位，既不得去，又不可死，于是有托以逃其生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206294_comment'></div>别离羁旅、流放忧畏之士顾无可乐，于是有托以快其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206294_comment'></div>私怪季氏无一于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206294_comment'></div>仕虽不达，而不以事经意，其于失得则轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206294_comment'></div>而亦好酒，无日不醉，苦心竭思，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1206294", 1206294, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>搜索肾胃</span>，如与世士出奇作新，夸多而斗捷，以角一时之名者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206294_comment'></div>与之久则涣然解，超然悟，而后知其非嗜味而嗜醉，非遣意而遣事也，其学陶氏、公孙氏者与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206294_comment'></div>元弼既殁，家无留藏，其子某索于里中，得诗若干首、文若干首而第次之，以请于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206294_comment'></div>余勤其成而尚其志也，为之序而藏之两家，使后之人知吾与若世好之如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206294_comment'></div>元弼名某，仕为许州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206294_comment'></div>元符二年八月癸巳，居士陈师道序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206294_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154707' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154707")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div id='poem_title_155148_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155148'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155148'>雨花风叶未宜春，私柳官渠白下门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155148'>每度清溪嘲短发，时容使席近芳樽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155148'>雄蜂雌蝶元非偶，野马游尘不佐鲲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155148'>若许成功当封赏<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：事具李待制席上篇。）</span>，请看子子与孙孙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155148'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155148_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155022?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送智叔令咸平</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155022")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155022'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155022'>二谢将能事，重阳只故台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155022'>固须冲节去，便恐带秋回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155022'>敏捷才无尽，铺张意有开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155022'>犹须记衰疾，书与雁同来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155022_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155022'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155022_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>持善序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年9月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206295")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206295'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206295'>世之力者有五：曰佛、曰法、曰善、曰恶、曰愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206295_comment'></div>善为至矣，然难行而易失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206295_comment'></div>士之始学，善新而恶熟，福轻而障厚，既难其大矣，而小又作辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206295_comment'></div>其为善岂惟其难，而魔力挠之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206295_comment'></div>其为不善岂惟其易，而业力使之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206295_comment'></div>是故先佛虽有种子之喻，又有汤冰焦谷之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206295_comment'></div>且堪忍之土，界则五浊，时则争斗，人则弊恶，缘则空，法则末，劫则陷，为之不亦难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206295_comment'></div>善出于习，而习不足恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206295_comment'></div>中人而下，善恶并作而更报，一出三涂，则失之尽矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206295_comment'></div>岂惟其然，异世则失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206295_comment'></div>声闻所不免，况于众乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206295_comment'></div>岂惟其然，异念则失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206295_comment'></div>前念之善，与念而尽，后念之恶，与念而兴，其失不亦易乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206295_comment'></div>虽然，为善有道，愿者善之所出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206295_comment'></div>愿之于善，犹业之于恶，能持其人，使不退失，故无愿则无善，无业则无恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206295_comment'></div>是以学者先愿而后善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206295_comment'></div>岂特善焉，虽法与佛，有不由此者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206295_comment'></div>故《华严》七地之菩萨，大愿力所摄，如来力所加，自善力所持，而得无生法忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206295_comment'></div>圣且假之人，况其下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206295_comment'></div>夫愿，本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206295_comment'></div>善与法、佛，条叶华实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206295_comment'></div>善非愿不生，佛非愿不成，更百化而弗渝，尽未来而不断，其为力大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206295_comment'></div>愿者心之用，则有自力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206295_comment'></div>以理为因，以先为證，则有他力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206295_comment'></div>具自他之力，不其宜乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206295_comment'></div>證至于佛，万法一空，其所不尽者愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206295_comment'></div>众生尽则愿尽，其无已乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206295_comment'></div>若夫善而无愿，与愿而非理，则为福而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206295_comment'></div>敬则贵，惠则富，世有贵富而不敬不惠者，以其无愿而失之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206295_comment'></div>虽然，士以私智而为愿，孰与效先之已试乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206295_comment'></div>先佛之愿莫大于妙德，莫要于普贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206295_comment'></div>十方同一时，住世之佛皆我所导而后成圣，不亦大乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206295_comment'></div>万德之行，出于十愿，不亦要乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206295_comment'></div>是以诸佛同赞而过见，菩萨自谓不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206295_comment'></div>元祐二年春，徐之东禅主者怀超梦出庭中，见二大师象系于木下，怪而问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206295_comment'></div>对曰：「此陈教授氏之物也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206295_comment'></div>是夏，师道始承命，至则馆于东禅，岂于二大士缘有素乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206295_comment'></div>绍圣二年之春，客东都，昼而燕坐，见大通禅师俯案指授，使具二愿，于是颇采《华严》、《宝积》而第次之，愿与信者而尽心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206295_comment'></div>元符二年九月二日，居士陈师道序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1206295_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_155237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155237'>后生守章句，不足供嗫嚅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155237'>一登吏部选，笔砚随扫除。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155237'>闭閤画眉妩，隔屋闻歌呼。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155237'>为邦得畿县，政密自计疏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155237'>宁书下下考，不奉急急符。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155237'>用意簿领外，筑室课典谟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155237'>桃李春事繁，轩窗昼景舒。<div id='poem_sentence_14_155237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_155237'>鸣屋鸠渴雨，窥帘燕哺雏。<div inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>须五斗轻千里，赖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>有斯人未肯忘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154833'></div><div showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与寇赵约丁塘看花寇以疾不赴有诗次其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154808'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154808'>早年学苦断过从，晚岁逢春意未穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154808'>欲共元刘争著语，不堪姚魏已随风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154808'>坐无上客席虚左，赠有英词囊不空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154808'>障日长须钓竿手，归来无计驻青骢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154808'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154808_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和寇十一同游城南阻雨还登寺山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154928")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154928'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154928'>雨阻游南步，泥留逐北情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154928'>稍看飞雾断，复作远山横。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154928'>野润膏新泽，楼明纳晚晴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154928'>归宜有佳思，纱帽压香英。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154928'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154928_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年3月</a>　在徐州家居，为魏衍母作墓铭。作品：《昌乐县君刘氏墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1206360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昌乐县君刘氏墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206360")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206360'>师道既铭魏君而葬，葬后再岁，君夫人卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206360_comment'></div>卒之三十六日，合于君之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206360_comment'></div>其葬速不及铭，岁之八月，其子衍始撰其行与事以请，将著之石而纳于隧，以明年之三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206360_comment'></div>师道既与为礼，遂略其词曰：刘氏之先，自咸阳而东，留彭城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206360_comment'></div>其后有昉，娶高氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206360_comment'></div>高有行，能以五行逆顺知人衰旺休咎，子孙数十人，谓夫人与其女孙必大，以归君与郑氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206360_comment'></div>君讳涛，卒朝奉郎，而郑丞秘书，皆有封邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206360_comment'></div>夫人事姑如母，视诸子如生，接微如上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206360_comment'></div>君为濮狱掾，里豪有狱，因乳医献大珠数万，夫人不取，遂绝医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206360_comment'></div>君彊直，数事忤上官，夫人谏曰：「子以禄为养，巽以行直，毋危言以近祸而忧其亲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206360_comment'></div>君氏富，群弟尽用且负，君又偿以禄，夫人不以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206360_comment'></div>君卒而家弊，亦不戚，视其子之学否与其客之贤不肖以喜忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206360_comment'></div>曰：「尔父常谓保身如保器，但虞伤缺耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206360_comment'></div>师道于是知君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206360_comment'></div>夫人元符元年秋从其子依沛之石氏，明年二月乙酉卒，年六十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206360_comment'></div>其歛与归，费出石氏，其葬也，邑人共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206360_comment'></div>夫人一子，衍也，来学，故其葬不以铭属人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206360_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1206360'>呜呼夫人，而有衍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206360_comment'></div>其学方兴，与其善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206360_comment'></div>身立名扬，亲则显也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206360_comment'></div>呜呼夫人，其无远也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1206360_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在徐州家居。作品：《三月二十二日榴花盛开戏作绝句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《和寇十一雨后登楼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷五、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《答寇十一惠朱樱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷五、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《双樱绝句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《谢赵生惠芍药三绝句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《寄邻绝句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《寄寇十一》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷七、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《和酬魏衍》<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155076'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155076'>邻里相望信不通，时因得句寄匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_155076_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_154940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154940?labeling=true' inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>怀一一逐归鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154940'>不忧寒饿成吾老，稍喜朝廷记此公。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154940'>梦每见君心已<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>了，不因新句觉情东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154940'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_154940'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_154940_0'>⑴ 宋注本及各本作离</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_154940_0'>⑵ 宋注本、高丽本、库注本作亦</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_154940_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在徐州家居，七月，除棣州教授。作品：《元符三年七月蒙恩复除棣学喜而成诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷五、《后山诗注补笺》卷一0。）</span>《与曾枢密书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山集》卷一0、《后山居士文集》卷一三。《后山居士文集》题作《与曾枢密启》）</span>《贺翰林曾学士书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山集》卷一0、《后山居士文集》卷一三。《后山居士文集》题作《贺翰林曾学士启》）</span><div id='poem_154816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元符三年七月蒙恩复除棣学喜而成诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154816")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154816'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154816'>老作诸侯客，贫为一饱谋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154816'>折腰真耐辱，捧檄敢轻投。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154816'>早作千年调，中怀万斛愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154816'>暮年随手尽，心事许溟鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154816'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154816_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上曾枢密书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206248")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206248'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206248'>月日，具官陈某西向再拜，献书于太尉六丈阁下：一去<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>门屏</span>，十年有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206248_comment'></div>平常不为问，非怠与外，以谓无益而不为尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206248_comment'></div>事有可言而复隐忍，然后为罪，则亦不敢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206248_comment'></div>夫天下之事，非阁下所得与，则非某所当言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206248_comment'></div>其在右府，且忧之大者，言之其亦可乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206248_comment'></div>西边用兵，五六年矣，远戍之卒，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>过期</span>不还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206248_comment'></div>人情及期则有归心，况又过之而后未期乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206248_comment'></div>以既动之心，而前有死伤之虞，内有羁旅暴露冻馁劳苦之害，后有乡邑亲爱之念，不亦危乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206248_comment'></div>然莫敢违异者，分定故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206248_comment'></div>鸟穷则攫，兽穷则搏，此虽常言，理有必至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206248_comment'></div>一人倡之，和者必众，东向而溃，何以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206248_comment'></div>夫事有曲直，人有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>违顺</span>，直之所在，胜之所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206248_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206248_comment'></div>人所顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206248_comment'></div>一旦发难，不过发内军以击之，无故兴师，积年不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206248_comment'></div>死伤之馀，思归而溃，而逆击之，则曲直有在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206248_comment'></div>窃恐溃者未至，发者不为用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206248_comment'></div>于是之时，在廷之人肯为天下国家以身捍之者谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206248_comment'></div>若其未有，可不计此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206248_comment'></div>某常所私忧窃叹者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206248_comment'></div>古之守国，本末并用，故建德而阻险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206248_comment'></div>开封无丘山川泽之阻，为四战之地，故太祖以兵为卫，畿内常用十四万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206248_comment'></div>今军卫多西戍，山东城郭一空，卒有盗贼乘间而作，冒州县、杀吏民、私货财、掠妇女、火室庐，乃其小者，不幸而有奸雄出焉，其成败孰得知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206248_comment'></div>忧之次也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206248_comment'></div>谈者必谓世方<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>平宁</span>，兵不足虞，人无奸雄，有不足畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206248_comment'></div>某不更远引<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>笔墨</span>所载，直以庆历以来耳目所及者明之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206248_comment'></div>恩、保两州之乱，庆之溃，皆卒也，王伦、张海、廖恩、王冲皆盗贼也，可谓平世而无之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206248_comment'></div>熙宁中士才再发，已自溃乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206248_comment'></div>于时某在秦中，闻乱兵所过，群小迎导，利其劫掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206248_comment'></div>王伦、张海行半天下，所至溃坏，守令或走或降，莫敢支梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206248_comment'></div>至出卫军，用边将，而官军所至，甚于盗贼，民至今谈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206248_comment'></div>从昔之乱，皆有奸雄，非为时而生，乃乱而后见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206248_comment'></div>平世伏而不出，遂以为无，则过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206248_comment'></div>某闻之景德、咸平之间，契丹岁入寇，游骑至山东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206248_comment'></div>齐有外镇，日莫尘起，人避走南山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206248_comment'></div>夜渴乏，既旦，视溪谷有冰雪，少年下食之，且取以上，众起争之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206248_comment'></div>有贾者出，止其众而坐之，率少年十馀辈而下，遍给坐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206248_comment'></div>且曰：「饥则奈何，孰从吾而取食」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206248_comment'></div>于是愿者数千人，斩木为兵，出屯镇中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206248_comment'></div>乃尽闭其外户，日以酒豕犒从者，夜则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>警捍</span>，旦暮饷山中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206248_comment'></div>三日而复，家不失一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206248_comment'></div>此与英、彭何异，而谓平世无之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206248_comment'></div>虽然，军溃盗起，一时之祸，所可虑者，分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206248_comment'></div>上之于下，可生可杀，可予可夺，而无违者，分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206248_comment'></div>分定则无所敢为，乱则无所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206248_comment'></div>如水之防，如薪之束，如兽之阱槛，其可失乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206248_comment'></div>一失则不复，断不可续，覆不可收，损不可完，物之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206248_comment'></div>此某之所深忧者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206248_comment'></div>谈者必谓还戍则备阙，寇来莫御，帅不任其责，某又谓其不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206248_comment'></div>戍有常数，今以拓土而增之尔，去其增则常也，尚何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206248_comment'></div>往者延安兵非不多，寇来不御，而仅自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206248_comment'></div>故善战者论将不论兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206248_comment'></div>夏人之来小，则其常，所虑者其大举尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206248_comment'></div>然方地数千里，外假邻阻，非可一日具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206248_comment'></div>师行千里，谋以时月，则孰不知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206248_comment'></div>帅者明其耳目而预为之备，何惮其来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206248_comment'></div>且虏短于攻，而不能久，人自持粮，后无馈运，往来不过数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206248_comment'></div>而我善守，寇至勿战，聚兵于内而清其野外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206248_comment'></div>内聚则寇不敢深，外清则深而不害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206248_comment'></div>使进不得战则沮，退无所掠则困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206248_comment'></div>以元昊之彊，数大入，才破塞门、金汤两城而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206248_comment'></div>国虽大而贫，兵虽多而散，以元昊之战胜而卒臣者，以数举而困也，况其弱乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206248_comment'></div>且以中国之盛大，灵武之举犹不能再，况于夷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206248_comment'></div>虽然，进筑不已则兵不得罢，盍先已之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206248_comment'></div>若谓可以制虏，则汉取阴山，匈奴过而恸哭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206248_comment'></div>开西域，发兵争之，故谓断其右臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206248_comment'></div>某居东，莫知今之可否，但闻诸路竞进，日夜奏功，而未闻西人举国而争，则必非其所急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206248_comment'></div>苟不能制其命，则老师费财，杀人盈野，何所用之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206248_comment'></div>若谓且筑且进，渐据横山，然后可制，则既数岁矣，横山安在耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206248_comment'></div>若复数岁，则诸将穷富极贵矣，人情得所欲，肯复出力蹈其所难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206248_comment'></div>则是横山终不可得，徒为将帅取富贵之资尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206248_comment'></div>横山，天险也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206248_comment'></div>下临平夏，存亡所系，虏必举国争之，恐亦未易得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206248_comment'></div>若谓今之所据即横山也，则某闻之，宥州在横山之上，南拒米脂三舍而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206248_comment'></div>今延安奏功广地四百里，则宥在其腹，然不云得宥州也，则四百里之广岂可信哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206248_comment'></div>胡地惟灵武、夏如内郡，地才可种荞、豆，且多沙碛，五月见青，七月而霜，岁才一收尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206248_comment'></div>银州草惟柴胡，萧关之外有落藜与咸杖，以此知其不宜五种也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206248_comment'></div>使可种，安得人实之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206248_comment'></div>若不徙民则募军，二者孰取焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206248_comment'></div>若取乎内，则空此以实彼，舍易而即艰，何益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206248_comment'></div>且辟土益广，则去府益远，平常缓请急报，卒不相及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206248_comment'></div>河东之患麟、府，世所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206248_comment'></div>若今所据可以制虏而不争者，非不敢，乃不能尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206248_comment'></div>虏虽蕞尔，然元昊用之以抗中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206248_comment'></div>其地与民固自若也，而今反不能争其所急者，非惜其力以有待，则无其人，不则诸部不为用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206248_comment'></div>若是，则某之忧有甚于前也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206248_comment'></div>今虏内弱外叛，而皇师临之，恐有乘危篡夺，以为奸雄之资，是复生一元昊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206248_comment'></div>故某常谓虏既弱矣，不复能抗中国，宜稍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/291/Comments/0")'>存立</span>，使假威命，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1206248", 1206248, "Clauses/293/Comments/0")'>临制</span>部族，压服奸豪，使不得发，奈何欲为之资乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206248_comment'></div>今使诸道尽据横山，而虏无奸雄乘时而起，一切如意，某之忧则又甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206248_comment'></div>赵文子曰：「苟非圣人，孰能内外无患，盍释楚以为外惧乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206248_comment'></div>夷狄之弱未有甚于今日者，可不忧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206248_comment'></div>今三边不战，士皆怯弱，独秦、晋数与虏角，犹可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206248_comment'></div>秦故西人，易东军如儿女子，而南平蛮、西南事羌，皆用秦卒以取胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206248_comment'></div>若又不战，卒有外患，何以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206248_comment'></div>昔岁之元昊、智高是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206248_comment'></div>窃谓西人不可无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206248_comment'></div>伏惟阁下股肱帝室，师表万邦，直道正词，天下称颂，日有传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206248_comment'></div>而独此无闻，岂未可以言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206248_comment'></div>言之，今其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206248_comment'></div>昔安、李两公皆有意于世，而各有失，安失之锐，李失之缓，故未及成功，而以毁去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206248_comment'></div>盖锐者不须时，缓者不及时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206248_comment'></div>时乎时乎，其可不知乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206248_comment'></div>《易》曰「书不尽言，言不尽意」，而况河山之外、翰墨之间乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206248_comment'></div>然以阁下英姿伟识，则区区之愚不待言而了，伏惟属意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206248_comment'></div>某再拜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206248_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_105_1206248'>「月日」至「阁下」：原无，据马刻本、库本及备要本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_105_1206248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1206248'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_104_1206248_0'>⑴ 《后山居士文集》卷九。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷一一九，《八代四六文钞》第三四册。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1206248_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1206280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206280?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺翰林曾学士启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206280")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206280'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206280'>内翰丈丈召从西掖，入直北门，岂惟儒者之荣，寔系朝廷之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206280_comment'></div>恭惟论思献纳之任，必须道德文学之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206280_comment'></div>不杂用于他材，故专收于夙望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206280_comment'></div>成命既下，欢声大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206280_comment'></div>虽图任未快于群情，而天下已被其阴赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206280_comment'></div>兄弟相望，乃平世之荣光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206280_comment'></div>鲁卫同升，亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1206280", 1206280, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>熙朝</span>之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206280_comment'></div>顾惟庸妄，早辱知怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206280_comment'></div>虽老弃诸侯，乃下流之自取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206280_comment'></div>而早亲文席，顾遗迹之尚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206280_comment'></div>仄闻新命之传，倍有舆人之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206280_comment'></div>秋阳尚炽，禁直云初，伏冀上为庙朝，精调寝寤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206280_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155294'>卧闻喧呼谁叩<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>阍，稚子往问鹿骇奔。<div "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>急手</span>疾口如翻盆<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作盆翻，据宋注本及各本乙）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155294'>冲风踏冻送七言，要令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_155294", 155294, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>寒屋</span>回春温。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155294'>是时积阴又黄昏，叫闹索火惊四邻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155294'>迩来<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_155294", 155294, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>结字</span>稳且匀，岂不见我参寥君。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155294'>嗟吾老矣心尚存，后来得子空马群。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155294'>径须赤手缚麒麟，四大海水一口吞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155294'>丈夫意气抗浮云，道逢其人两手分，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_155294", 155294, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>妒妇</span>拊膺王右军。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_155294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155294'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_155294_0'>⑴ 宋注本及各本作叫</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155294_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1206282' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206282' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206282?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上棣州守启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206282")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206282_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206282'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206282'>祗荷误恩，复司外学，方承大庇，徒切至怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206282_comment'></div>伏惟某官清白承家，文明烛物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206282_comment'></div>出入省寺，已宣布于风声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206282_comment'></div>选用循良，足慰安于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1206282", 1206282, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>疲瘵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206282_comment'></div>顾兹海右，方报政成，岂意妄庸，获奉条教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206282_comment'></div>青衫白首，尚怀五斗之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206282_comment'></div>黄卷赤文，莫副诸儒之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206282_comment'></div>倾瞻之素，翰墨奚伸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206282_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与交代启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206283")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206283'>永惟平日，讲闻声烈之详；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206283_comment'></div>岂意莫年，获托交承之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206283_comment'></div>兴言及此，为慰可量！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206283_comment'></div>伏惟某官学以成家，德方名世，抗诸儒而著节，度两汉以修文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206283_comment'></div>方圣君侧席之求，乃贤者汇征之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206283_comment'></div>某已戒行舟，方趋宾次，倾瞻之切，翰墨奚伸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206283_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206284' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与棣州幕职启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206284")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206284'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206284'>蒙误恩之逮下，还旧贯以起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206284_comment'></div>愧非文学之英，复冒师儒之宠，永惟侥倖，有愧心颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206284_comment'></div>伏惟某官婉画佐州，弥文饰吏，士有登门之峻，宠深入幕之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206284_comment'></div>向德有年，趋风在即，倾瞻之切，翰墨奚伸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206284_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155111' -----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a1a1c1cad06748828f08cb3a30dbdeac_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a1a1c1cad06748828f08cb3a30dbdeac");'><span id='a1a1c1cad06748828f08cb3a30dbdeac_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>，14岁</div><div id='a1a1c1cad06748828f08cb3a30dbdeac' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　陈师道父陈琪自冀州度支使迁大理寺丞，师道或随任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='51948db68aca454e8cfc7488c800c61d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("51948db68aca454e8cfc7488c800c61d");'><span id='51948db68aca454e8cfc7488c800c61d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1070')">1069-1070年</a>，18-19岁</div><div id='51948db68aca454e8cfc7488c800c61d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　陈师道随父居开封，时王安石已执政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　陈师道随父居开封。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5f692b7c31bc41faaa535ca39411f28e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5f692b7c31bc41faaa535ca39411f28e");'><span id='5f692b7c31bc41faaa535ca39411f28e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>，30岁</div><div id='5f692b7c31bc41faaa535ca39411f28e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>　陈师道至开封，晤颜复，谒曾巩，时晁补之亦在开封，有诗赠答。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年7月5日</a>　为王安国作文集序。作品：《王平甫文集后序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一六。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚，故系于此年，地点则待考。）</span><div id='poem_1206293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王平甫文集后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年7月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206293")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206293'>欧阳永叔谓梅圣俞曰：「世谓诗能穷人，非诗之穷，穷则工也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206293_comment'></div>圣俞以诗名家，仕不前人，年不后人，可谓穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206293_comment'></div>其同时有王平甫，临川人也，年过四十始名，荐书群下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206293_comment'></div>历年未几，复解章绶归田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206293_comment'></div>其穷甚矣，而文义蔚然，又能于诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206293_comment'></div>惟其穷愈甚，故其得愈多，信所谓人穷而后工也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206293_comment'></div>虽然，天之命物，用而不全，实者不华，渊者不陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206293_comment'></div>物之不全，物之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206293_comment'></div>尽天下之美，则于贵富不得兼而有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206293_comment'></div>诗之穷人，又可信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206293_comment'></div>方平甫之时，其志抑而不伸，其才积而不发，其号位势力不足动人，而人闻其声，家有其书，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1206293", 1206293, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>旁行</span>于一时而下达于千世，虽其怨敌不敢议也，则诗能达人矣，未见其穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206293_comment'></div>夫士之行世，穷达不足论，论其所传而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206293_comment'></div>平甫孝悌于家，信于友，勇于义而好仁，不特文之可传也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206293_comment'></div>向使平甫用力于世，荐声诗于郊庙，施典策于朝廷，而事负其言，后戾其前，则并其可传而弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206293_comment'></div>平生之学可谓勤矣，天下之誉可谓盛矣，一朝而失之，岂不哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206293_comment'></div>南丰先生既叙其文以诏学者，先生之没，彭城陈师道因而伸之，以通于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206293_comment'></div>诚愚不敏，其能使人后其所利而隆其所弃者耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206293_comment'></div>因先生之言以致其志，又以自励云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206293_comment'></div>元丰四年七月五日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206293_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='797235604a1d4d7f9f08e4e2b8a8936b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("797235604a1d4d7f9f08e4e2b8a8936b");'><span id='797235604a1d4d7f9f08e4e2b8a8936b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1084')">1082-1084年</a>，31-33岁</div><div id='797235604a1d4d7f9f08e4e2b8a8936b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　陈师道携家居开封，以授徒自给，有时并由母舅庞元英及岳父郭槩接济。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　陈师道居开封，四月十一日，曾巩卒于江宁府，陈师道作挽诗二首，又作妾薄命二首以见意。作品：《南丰先生挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四。）</span>《妾薄命二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_154952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南丰先生挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154952")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154952'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154952'>早弃人间事，真从地下游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154952'>丘原无起日，江汉有东流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154952'>身世<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_154952", 154952, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>从违</span>里，功名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>取次休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154952'>不应须礼乐，始作后程仇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154952'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_154952'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_154952_0'>⑴ 高丽本、库注本作言</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_154952_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_154951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_154951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154951'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154951'>精爽回长夜，衣冠出广庭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154951'>勋庸留琬琰，形像付丹青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154951'>道丧馀篇翰，人亡更典刑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154951'>侯芭才一足，白首太玄经。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154951'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154951_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>妾薄命二首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155234")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155234_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_155234_0'>① 为曾南丰作（题注原缺，据各本补）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155234'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155234'>主家十二楼，一身当三千。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155234'>古来妾薄命，事主不尽年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155234'>起舞为主寿，相送南阳阡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155234'>忍著主衣裳，为人作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_155234", 155234, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>春妍</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155234'>有声当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_155234", 155234, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>彻天</span>，有泪当彻泉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155234'>死者恐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_155234", 155234, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>无知</span>，妾身长自怜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155234'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_155234_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155233?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155233'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155233'>叶落风不起，山空花自红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155233'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_155233", 155233, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>捐世</span>不待老，惠妾无其终。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155233'>一死尚可忍，百岁何当穷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155233'>天地岂不宽，妾身自不容。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155233'>死者如有知，杀身以相从。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155233'>向来歌舞处<span class='inlineComment2'>（各本作地）</span>，夜雨鸣寒蛩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155233'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_155233_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年8月10日</a>　陈师道居开封，为钱塘思白堂作记。作品：《思白堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1206331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206331?labeling=true' target='_blank'>思白堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰六年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年8月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206331")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206331_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206331'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206331'>元丰四年，予游吴，过秀，见林侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206331_comment'></div>侯家于苏而宦学于杭，能道其江湖山林之美、游览之乐，而甚爱思白堂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206331_comment'></div>其秋八月，就舍钱塘，问思白之堂而往观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206331_comment'></div>临渊而望，西山楼观出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206331_comment'></div>渊昧而林茂，鱼鸟乐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206331_comment'></div>江海山泽林庐之气相错，风林水麓鸟兽之声相乱，而雨旸寒暑昼夜之变不齐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206331_comment'></div>慨然怀顾昔人之风声，而自乐一时之得意，宜侯之甚爱而不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206331_comment'></div>而耆老豪杰文学之士，请载之石，以侈其赐，予未有以辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206331_comment'></div>湖之东州保宁之寺，故唐刺史白公居易燕游之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206331_comment'></div>近时律师某治其后堂而请于侯，于是名之，以致其思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206331_comment'></div>又大书之以表其处，而思白之号，闻于吴中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206331_comment'></div>夫前世<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1206331", 1206331, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>游居</span>之士有传于后者多矣，独有意于白公何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206331_comment'></div>进则效其忠，退则存其身，仁以成政，文以成言，此公之行，而侯与士大夫之所思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206331_comment'></div>公为刺史，知民之啬于水也，筑塘浚井，其利至今，岂特士大夫之思哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206331_comment'></div>夫怨其所恶，思其所好，人之所同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206331_comment'></div>士以德言，民以功利，其所异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206331_comment'></div>而吏无全能，故上下之论不一，若公则思者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206331_comment'></div>士之为善诚无事于言，而行终其身，功尽于事，必待言而后传，则又不可已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206331_comment'></div>公言见于书，行见于史，故今有以思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206331_comment'></div>此言之不亡，而记之所以作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206331_comment'></div>林侯常以集贤校理通判秀州，今为尚书礼部郎中，其文学行治略与公等，后之人又将思之，其可辞乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206331_comment'></div>明年而余北归，又明年而为之记，不知余文使人思之如两侯否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206331_comment'></div>六年八月十日，彭城陈师道记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1206331_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　陈师道子陈丰生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　五月，陈师道岳父郭槩改官提点成都府路刑狱，师道妻及子女随槩入蜀，陈师道本人奉母留居开封。作品：《送外舅郭大夫槩西川提刑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一。）</span>《送内》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一。）</span>《别三子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_155253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155253")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155253'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155253'>丈人东南来，复作西南去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155253'>连年万里别，更觉贫贱苦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155253'>王事有期程，亲年当喜惧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155253'>畏与妻子别，已复迫<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_4_155253'>何者最可怜，儿生未知父。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155253'>盗贼非人情，蛮夷正狼顾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155252'>麀麌顾其子，燕雀各有<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>随。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155252'>与子为夫妇，五年三别离。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155252'>儿女岂不怀，母老妹已笄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155252'>父子各从母，可喜亦可悲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155252'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_155252", 155252, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>关河</span>万里道，子去何当归。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155252'>三岁不可道，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_155252", 155252, id='poem_content_155210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155210'>夫妇死同穴，父子贫贱离。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155210'>天下宁有此，昔闻今见之。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155210'>母前三子后，熟视不得追。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155210'>嗟乎胡不仁，使我至于斯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155210'>有女初束发，已知生离悲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155210'>枕我不肯起，畏我从此辞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155210'>大儿学语言，拜揖未胜衣。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155210'>唤耶我欲去，此语那可思。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155210'>小儿襁褓间，抱负有母慈。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155210'>汝哭犹在耳，我怀人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_155210", 155210, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　陈师道改字无己，黄庭坚为作字序，改字后，原字履常仍旧并用。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　傅尧俞闻师道名，请秦观为介，先来见，师道答拜，是为二人相识之始。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　陈师道在开封。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='21cae9aed7f8441f8a9d3330eeb3b099_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("21cae9aed7f8441f8a9d3330eeb3b099");'><span id='21cae9aed7f8441f8a9d3330eeb3b099_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1087')">1085-1087年</a>，34-36岁</div><div id='21cae9aed7f8441f8a9d3330eeb3b099' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　五六月间，知枢密院事章惇嘱秦观示意师道往见之，将荐于朝，师道辞不往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　作诗寄岳父郭槩。作品：《寄外舅郭大夫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。此诗任渊《年谱》系元丰七年甲子元丰八年乙丑，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_155055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄外舅郭大夫二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155055")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155055'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155055'>巴蜀通归使，妻孥且旧居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155055'>深知报消息，不忍问何如。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155055'>身健何妨远，情亲未肯疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155055'>功名欺老病，泪尽数行书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155055'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155055_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155272?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155272'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155272'>丈人鲁诸生，明刑如皋陶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155272'>幸宽右顾忧，未惜一身遥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155272'>西南万里行，可以断<span class='inlineComment2'>（赵本、库本作绝）</span>绳桥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155272'>慎勿用<span class='inlineComment2'>（各本作冠）</span>惠文，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_155272", 155272, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>神母</span>仁如尧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155272'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年9月</a>　在开封，寓居东南门外佛寺。作品：《城南寓居二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_155239' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155239' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155239?labeling=true' target='_blank'>城南寓居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155239")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155239_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_155239_0'>① 原作二首，其二“潭潭光明殿”与卷四《秋怀十首》之十同，今删</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155239'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155239'>游子暮何归，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_155239", 155239, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>韦杜</span>城南村。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155239'>秋水深可测，挽衣踏行云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155239'>道暗失归处，栖鸟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>故不喧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155239'>牛羊闭篱落，稚子犹在门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155239'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155239'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_155239_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本、张本作乌</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155239_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　在开封，思念儿子，作诗。作品：《忆少子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。此诗任渊《年谱》系元丰七年甲子元丰八年乙丑，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_155169' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155169' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155169?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆少子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155169")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155169_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155169'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155169'>端也早<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_155169", 155169, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>丰下</span>，岁晚未可量。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155169'>我老不自食，安得如我长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155169'>呱呱弃不子，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_155169", 155169, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>退省</span>未始忘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155169'>吾母亦念我，与尔宁相望。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155169'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155169_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　陈师道居开封，早春，张耒来开封，旋别去，是为陈张相识之始。作品：《答张文潜书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一0。）</span><div id='poem_1206243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答张文潜书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206243")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206243'>师道启：近者足下来京师，不鄙其愚，辱贶以文，卒卒一再见，怀不得吐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206243_comment'></div>既别，欲一致问，因以自效，方事之不间，竟后足下，大以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206243_comment'></div>及读足下书，乃仆所欲言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206243_comment'></div>君子之所存，去人不远，惟设之于仆为不当耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206243_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206243_comment'></div>足下诚知我矣，亦既爱之矣，不识足下何从而得之，其得之于人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206243_comment'></div>其有以自得之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206243_comment'></div>得之于人耶，誉者可信，则毁者又可信矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206243_comment'></div>有以自得之耶，则仆言未效而迹未接，窃有疑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206243_comment'></div>岂足下使人可疑，乃仆之不敏不能不疑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206243_comment'></div>古盖有之，目逆而道存，而仆不足当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206243_comment'></div>以仆之愚，有以知足下，而谓足下何从而得之，仆过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206243_comment'></div>夫众言却金，三人成虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206243_comment'></div>仆惧足下有时不自信而信人，不待人毁而自毁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206243_comment'></div>仆以小人之怀为君子之心，则又过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206243_comment'></div>然所以言者，虽君子不可不戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206243_comment'></div>足下悯仆无以事亲、畜妻子，宜从下科，以幸斗食，疑仆好恶与人异情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206243_comment'></div>足下于仆至矣，仆何以得之，何以受之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206243_comment'></div>仆家以仕为业，舍仕则技穷矣，故仆之于仕，如瘖者之溺，声气不动而手足乱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206243_comment'></div>世徒见其忍而不发，遂以为好恶异人，此殆谈者过情，听者过信耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206243_comment'></div>虽然，仆病且老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206243_comment'></div>目有黑子而昏华，瘯瘰侠于颈领隐起而未溃，气伏于胸腹之间下上不时，痔形于下体者十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206243_comment'></div>志彊而形惫，年未既而老及之，足下虽欲进之，而仆不能勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206243_comment'></div>闰月甲子诏以河内公为相，是时自九月不雨，有司传诏未竟而雨，贵贱贤不肖下至房室女子，欢然相庆，天人之意如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206243_comment'></div>仆方卧，闻之起立，尚可勉耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206243_comment'></div>足下视此时如何，仆独得不勉耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206243_comment'></div>羊鼎之侧，饥者吐舌，但未染指耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206243_comment'></div>足下欲与仆居，将坐仆而沐熏之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206243_comment'></div>岂意其逃世而加束缚焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206243_comment'></div>抑爱之过厚而欲常常见之与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206243_comment'></div>李耽家于濑乡，庄休老于蒙，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1206243", 1206243, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>田邑</span>之间，复有昔时怀器而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1206243", 1206243, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>隐处</span>者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206243_comment'></div>愿一览焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206243_comment'></div>仆于书如贪者之嗜利，未尝厌其欲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206243_comment'></div>谯祁氏多书，称号外府、太清老氏之藏室，愿与足下尽心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206243_comment'></div>春益暄，惟为道重慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206243_comment'></div>师道再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1206243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　陈师道居开封。作品：《绝句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷一二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年2月1日</a>　为秦观作字序。作品：《秦少游字叙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一六。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦少游字序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206303")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206303'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206303'>熙宁、元丰之间，眉苏公之守徐，余以民事太守，间见如客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206303_comment'></div>扬秦子过焉，置醴备乐，如师弟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206303_comment'></div>其时余病卧里中，闻其行道雍容，逆者旋目，论说伟辩，坐者属耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206303_comment'></div>世以此奇之而亦以此疑之，惟公以为杰士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206303_comment'></div>是后数岁，从吴归，见于广陵逆旅之家，夜半语未卒，别去，余亦以谓当建侯万里外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206303_comment'></div>元丰之末，余客东都，秦子从东来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206303_comment'></div>别数岁矣，其容充然，其口隐然，余惊焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206303_comment'></div>以问秦子，曰：「往吾少时，如杜牧之彊志盛气，好大而见奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206303_comment'></div>读兵家书，乃与意合，谓功誉可力致，而天下无难事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206303_comment'></div>顾今二虏有可胜之势，愿效至计，以行天诛，回幽、夏之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1206303", 1206303, "Clauses/39/Comments/1")'>故墟</span>，吊唐、晋之遗人，流声无穷，为计不朽，岂不伟哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206303_comment'></div>于是字以太虚，以导吾志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206303_comment'></div>今吾年至而虑易，不待蹈险而悔及之，愿还四方之事，归老邑里，如马少游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206303_comment'></div>于是字以少游，以识吾过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206303_comment'></div>尝试以语公，又以为可，于子何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206303_comment'></div>余以谓取善于人，以成其身，君子伟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206303_comment'></div>且夫二子或进以经世，或退以存身，可与为仁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206303_comment'></div>然行者难工，处者易持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206303_comment'></div>牧之之智得，不若少游之拙失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206303_comment'></div>子以倍人之才，学益明矣，犹屈意于少游，岂过直以矫曲耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206303_comment'></div>子年益高，德益大，余将屡惊焉，不一再而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206303_comment'></div>虽然，以子之才，虽不效于世，世不舍子，余意子终有万里行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206303_comment'></div>如余之愚，莫宜于世，乃当守丘墓，保田里，力农以奉公上，谨身以训闾巷，生称善人，死表于道，曰「处士陈君之墓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206303_comment'></div>或者天祚以年，见子功遂名成，奉身以还，王侯将相，高车大马，祖行帐饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206303_comment'></div>于是乘庳御驽，候子上东门外，举酒相属，成公知人之名，以为子贺，盖自此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206303_comment'></div>元祐元年二月一日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1206303_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　作诗寄岳父郭槩。作品：《寄外舅郭大夫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_155055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄外舅郭大夫二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155055")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155055'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155055'>巴蜀通归使，妻孥且旧居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155055'>深知报消息，不忍问何如。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155055'>身健何妨远，情亲未肯疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155055'>功名欺老病，泪尽数行书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155055_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155055'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155055_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155272?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155272'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155272'>丈人鲁诸生，明刑如皋陶。<div
