id='poem_sentence_3_155272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155272'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　春，郭槩为苏辙奏劾，罢西川提刑任，师道妻及子女自蜀归开封。作品：《示三子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_155177' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155177' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155177?labeling=true' target='_blank'>示三子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155177")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155177_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155177'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155177'>去远即相忘，归近不可忍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155177'>儿女已在眼，眉目略不省。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155177'>喜极不得语，泪尽方一哂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155177'>了知不是梦，忽忽心未稳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155177'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155177_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　本年，晁补之为太学正，张耒为太学录，同荐师道为太学录，不就。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　闻徐积之名，作书托门人江端礼持往谒徐，徐托江转致谢意，未作答书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　居开封，作诗。作品：《暑雨》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_155116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暑雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155116")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155116_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155116'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155116'>密雨吹不断，贫居常闭门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155116'>东溟容有限，西极更能存。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155116'>束湿炊悬釜，翻床补坏垣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155116'>倒身无著处，呵手不成温。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155116'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155116_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年8月</a>　居开封，为关氏作《二亭记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206332")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206332'>居则行其仁，仕则行其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206332_comment'></div>家非仁不亲，君臣之际又有义焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206332_comment'></div>仁始于身，内有以守，同其乐于天，外有以安，同其好于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206332_comment'></div>故为宫室苑囿以燕其居，车马器服以效其用，宾射燕享以广其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206332_comment'></div>故能群天下而世守焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206332_comment'></div>钱塘关氏于其居之右地积土为坂，伐石为坛，而蓺以药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206332_comment'></div>坂之下有甘井焉，挟以二室，左竹右木，断而不斲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206332_comment'></div>命其坂曰「药坂」，坛曰「芝坛」，井曰「丹井」，左曰「巢亭」，右曰「节亭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206332_comment'></div>自是关氏之父兄子弟仕而休者，与夫学而未仕者，朝夕在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206332_comment'></div>府县之吏，乡邑之老，与夫四方之过宾间从其游，所乐虽异，而各有得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206332_comment'></div>呜呼，可谓仁其身矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206332_comment'></div>引而近之，守莫固焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206332_comment'></div>推而外之，政莫善焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206332_comment'></div>关氏为吴大家，世有彦士，其宦于朝者三人，仕于州县者四人，处而学者又十有几人，因而大之，其兴乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206332_comment'></div>蜀方士李翁曰，石有玉可攻，甘井可化丹砂，而未试也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206332_comment'></div>后有贪者，将剥石以贾玉，竭井以市丹砂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206332_comment'></div>关氏盛衰，于是见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206332_comment'></div>作亭之明年，关氏之良彦瞻来京师，以告其寮友、游旧，于是士大夫之能诗者，皆为赋之，而属余为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206332_comment'></div>元祐元年八月丙戌，彭城陈师道记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206332_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年9月</a>　九月，司马光卒，陈师道有挽诗三首。作品：《丞相温公挽诗三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_154830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丞相温公挽词三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154830")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154830'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154830'>恭默思良弼，诗书正<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_154830", 154830, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>百工</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154830'>事多违谢傅，天遽夺杨公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154830'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_154830", 154830, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>一代风流</span>尽，三师礼数崇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154830'>若无天下议，美恶并成空。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154830'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154830_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154829?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154829'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154829'>百姓归周老，三年待鲁儒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154829'>世<span class='inlineComment2'>（各本作时）</span>方随日化，身已要人扶。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154829'>玉几虽来晚，明堂讫授图。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154829'>心知死诸葛，终不羡曹蜍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154829'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154829_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154828?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154828'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154828'>少学真成己，中年托著书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154828'>辍耕扶日月，起废极吹嘘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154828'>得志宁论晚，成功不愿馀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154828'>一为天下恸，不敢爱吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154828'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154828_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　本年，曾与黄叔达同谒法云禅师，夜归，过李公麟，公麟为作夜归图，邢居实为作诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　居开封，为江端礼作《御书记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一五。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御书记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206344")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206344'>仁宗皇帝御书，两纸四字，其文曰「善法行政」，其玺文曰「帝录」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206344_comment'></div>皇祐、嘉祐之间，以赐其臣江休复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206344_comment'></div>于是休复为集贤校理、御试详定官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206344_comment'></div>休复以文义诵说，明习世务，奉使有绩，列于名臣，遂蒙显扬，宠以翰墨，归藏于家而世守之，其为平生之观，学者之荣至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206344_comment'></div>休复后为刑部郎中、修起居注以卒，其孙端礼以示臣师道，使记载皇帝所以照临江氏，假宠子孙，明示来今，臣盖不得辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206344_comment'></div>臣愚敬惟皇帝之于书极矣，在位四十馀年，外被四夷，下逮百世，口耳所传，纸墨所载，德政道化有不胜言，其不习而能者，岂圣人优为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206344_comment'></div>臣亦不敢赞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206344_comment'></div>臣生于皇祐四年，被蒙恩泽，上下田里，不畏不夭，至于成人，而曾不得望前驱之尘，蹈后车之躅，臣不胜至恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206344_comment'></div>乃今幸得伏览圣制，见至人之用心，附于不忘，臣亦与有荣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206344_comment'></div>端礼学而不息，文而不露，能世其家，将复受赐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206344_comment'></div>元祐元年闰月己丑，徐州彭城县王乡任化里臣陈师道昧死谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　居开封，作诗赠二苏。作品：《赠二苏公》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷三、《后山诗注补笺》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_155308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠二苏公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155308")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155308'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155308'>岷峨之山中巴江，桂椒楠栌枫柞樟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155308'>青金黄玉丹砂良，兽皮鸟羽不足当。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155308'>异人间出骇四方，严王陈李司马扬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155308'>一翁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_155308", 155308, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>二季</span>对相望，奇宝横道骥伏<span class='inlineComment2'>（各本作服）</span>箱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155308'>谁其识者有欧阳，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_155308", 155308, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>大科</span>异等固其常。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155308'>小却盛之白玉堂，典谟颂雅<span class='inlineComment2'>（各本作雅颂）</span>用所长。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155308'>度越周汉登虞唐，千载之下有素王。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155308'>平陈郑毛视荒荒，后生不作诸老亡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155308'>文体变化未可量，万口一律如吃羌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155308'>妖狐幻人犬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>陆梁，虎豹却走逢牛羊。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155308'>上帝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_155308", 155308, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>惠顾</span>祓不祥，天门夜下龙虎章。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155308'>前驱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_155308", 155308, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>吴回</span>后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_155308", 155308, "Clauses/22/Comments/1")'>炎皇</span>，绛旂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_155308", 155308, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>丹毂</span>朱冠裳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155308'>从以甲胄万鬼行，乘风纵燎无留藏。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155308'>天高地下日月光，授公以柄扶病伤。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155308'>士如稻苗待公秧，临流不渡公为航。<div id='poem_sentence_14_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_155308'>如大医王治膏肓，外證已解中尚彊。<div id='poem_sentence_15_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_155308'>探囊一试<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_155308", 155308, "Clauses/32/Comments/1")'>黄昏汤</span><sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，一洗十年<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_155308", 155308, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>新学</span>肠。<div id='poem_sentence_16_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_155308'>老生塞口不敢尝，向来狂杀今尚狂，请公别试囊中方。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_155308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155308'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_155308_0'>⑴ 高丽本、赵本、四库本、库注本作大</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_155308_0'>⑵ 高丽本、库注本任渊校：一本云愿借上古黄昏汤</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155308_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　居开封，为曾巩作挽词。作品：《南丰先生挽词二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_154952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_154984'>濠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>梁初得意，阙里旧论诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154984'>晚岁何多难，经年始一辞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154984'>淮人饥馑后，良吏拊循时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154984'>欲托山阳簿，翁归不受私<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：南丰之子绾为山阳簿。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154984'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_154984'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_154984_0'>⑴ 原作豪，据四库本、库注本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_154984_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1206244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答江端礼书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206244")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206244'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206244'>师道启：学始于身而成于性，欲善其身而不明于善，所谓徒善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206244_comment'></div>徒善者非善之正也，是故学者所以明善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206244_comment'></div>学，外也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206244_comment'></div>思，内也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206244_comment'></div>学以佐行，思以佐学，古之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206244_comment'></div>若其自得，则在子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206244_comment'></div>士之所戒，其惟名乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206244_comment'></div>声实相从，如影之于形，短长曲直，惟形之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206244_comment'></div>无实之名，黎人败焉，善人畏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206244_comment'></div>得且畏之，况求之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206244_comment'></div>言以述志，文以成言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206244_comment'></div>约之以义，行之以信，近则致其用，远则致其传，文之质也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206244_comment'></div>大以为小，小以为大，简而不约，盈而不馀，文之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206244_comment'></div>正心完气，广之以学，斯至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206244_comment'></div>辱问非所及，敬诵所闻，足下其择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206244_comment'></div>仆之不敏，勤无成能，惟于修文，略有师法，愧无异闻，虚辱盛意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206244_comment'></div>若曰量子以为教，如医之量药以当病，如工之量材以当用，子曾子盖能之矣，仆非其任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206244_comment'></div>嗟乎，子之不逢夫子也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206244_comment'></div>与仆游者众矣，莫有问焉，子何问之下耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206244_comment'></div>嗟乎，夫子之失子也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206244_comment'></div>尚幸来临，愿言其详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206244_comment'></div>师道再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1206244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_154703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154703'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154703'>色轻花更艳，体弱香自永。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154703'>玉质金作裳，山明风弄影。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154703'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154703_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='13b269b217d842c1b86b00812d16878c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("13b269b217d842c1b86b00812d16878c");'><span id='13b269b217d842c1b86b00812d16878c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，43岁</div><div id='13b269b217d842c1b86b00812d16878c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　赴开封，至吏部注官，得监海陵酒税，未赴任。在开封时，曾偕友往访吕希哲。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9b1dc1ef600f4c36ba71ce3bfa00d461_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9b1dc1ef600f4c36ba71ce3bfa00d461");'><span id='9b1dc1ef600f4c36ba71ce3bfa00d461_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>，44岁</div><div id='9b1dc1ef600f4c36ba71ce3bfa00d461' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　早春，居开封，由监海陵酒税改官江州彭泽县令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年2月17日</a>　居开封，应法云寺慧严禅师面请为张居士作墓表。作品：《张居士墓表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1206364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张居士墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206364")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206364'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206364'>居士张隆，字君道，苏之吴人，以书计为县簿史，乐声色酒博以自放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206364_comment'></div>年二十八，有名比丘谕以罪福真幻，卒然悔悟，委家绝世，专意释氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206364_comment'></div>衣粗食淡，奉菩萨戒，滋久益严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206364_comment'></div>从雍熙道场元智法师授《华严》义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206364_comment'></div>手具疏抄，礼《华严》、《法华》、《楞严经》《、起信论》、《法界观》、《清凉抄疏》及他经凡数百卷，字一致敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206364_comment'></div>又以梁忏为众礼佛十有一焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206364_comment'></div>其称佛菩萨号每以百万数，率众供僧每以千计，言听事治，人以为能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206364_comment'></div>曰：「吾非自效，为作龙华之因尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206364_comment'></div>日再至，讲所习天台、贤首二教，退则礼诵跪绕，阅《大藏经》，口不绝声，身不旷礼，夜尽三更，迨五鼓而兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206364_comment'></div>每三八日会家众供佛，说教以终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206364_comment'></div>熙宁六年十月既望，年四十八矣，且有厌世语，遂与其子宗永别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206364_comment'></div>既讲还，未至，觉背痛，至则趺座，诵观音号，掖以如寝，及席而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206364_comment'></div>常曰「吾死用浮图法」，于是火焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206364_comment'></div>明年冬至，葬县之南里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206364_comment'></div>娶闻氏，产四男子，圭、崇、宗永、湜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206364_comment'></div>初，居士以两子事浮图，师既卒，崇复家，而宗永遂为比丘，号惠严大师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206364_comment'></div>初，居士奇其子，故舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206364_comment'></div>自其幼时，有胜会必与俱，以导其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206364_comment'></div>其后往来江湖间，事圆通禅师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206364_comment'></div>圆通来居东都法云，以为修造主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206364_comment'></div>于是合众施为殿藏门寮，前庖后寝，凡费六千万，更十年而后成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206364_comment'></div>长者廖宁一见施千万，为三佛、六菩萨、十八大士、群从卫之象，其所为必极天下之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206364_comment'></div>既成而去，于是惠严之名行于方内，相传以为神奇而不知其所馀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206364_comment'></div>顾其中有大焉，而未试也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206364_comment'></div>语曰知子其父，果哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206364_comment'></div>初，居士葬不铭，余与惠严好，于其别，为次其行，使归镵诸石，以表其阡，以慰其乡之思，以启后人，其勿坏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1206364_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='71c41b51a8044642acf4af06b9db8c07_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("71c41b51a8044642acf4af06b9db8c07");'><span id='71c41b51a8044642acf4af06b9db8c07_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>，45岁</div><div id='71c41b51a8044642acf4af06b9db8c07' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　往雍丘省视外祖庞籍墓，至陈留，宿深明阁。作品：《宿深明阁二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_155050' class='_poem'><div inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，潮回趁急流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155009'>平生湖海兴，日夜逐行舟。<div class='inlineComment2'>（宋注本及各本作膺期符宝历）</span>，锡号焕皇扉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155028'>日月尧同数，讴歌启与归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155028'>伤心五云去，不见六龙飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155028'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155028_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206362?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仲父荣州资官尉陈君墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206362")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206362'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206362'>仲父讳某，字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206362_comment'></div>先大父为怀州，有相者过之，使视诸子，谓君不宜仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206362_comment'></div>庆历中，君以任为试秘书省校书郎，调荣之资官尉，不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206362_comment'></div>京兆之鄠、临潼主簿，举监环之折博务，皆不终，谓君非不仕，特不宜尔，何妙耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206362_comment'></div>然则形骨可以知其贵贱，气色可以知其咎休，而荀子非之何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206362_comment'></div>元丰几年，年五十有几而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206362_comment'></div>有一子，曰师中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206362_comment'></div>三女，嫁李某、邵敏脩、张某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206362_comment'></div>敏脩今为临淄主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206362_comment'></div>建中靖国元年五月某日，叔父前昆山丞珣葬于彭城吕栅之大茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206362_comment'></div>君娶解氏，光禄卿程之女，亦不终，故其葬不祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206362_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1206362'>昏宦不卒，则归之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206362_comment'></div>如何不淑，又不得年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206362_comment'></div>兄弟之怀，葬从先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206362_comment'></div>归安其居，宜尔子孙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1206362_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>季父上骑都尉陈通直墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206363")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206363'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206363'>先大父有五子，君其季也，讳某，字粹父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206363_comment'></div>皇祐元年，大父为三司盐铁副使，行视河还而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206363_comment'></div>仁宗怀之，官其一子七品京官，复诏有司毋以为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206363_comment'></div>君由是为将作监簿，迁太常奉礼郎，大理评事，卫尉、大理两丞，太子中舍，改通直郎，监杭、楚、沂三州之酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206363_comment'></div>元丰四年，年四十矣，卒于下邳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206363_comment'></div>娶庄氏，永和县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206363_comment'></div>生三女，嫁段辩、耿寿恺、高友谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206363_comment'></div>大父有世材，故其子皆长于吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206363_comment'></div>君所试小，未足观能否，亦无传闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206363_comment'></div>然杭于今号繁剧，视天府，而孙威敏、沈文通两公为前后守之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206363_comment'></div>某至杭，问其所治，莫能称说君事，沈公独能记之，由是不试知其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206363_comment'></div>君无子，其兄昆山丞珣用建中靖国元年五月几日，葬于彭城吕栅，祔先兆之丙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206363_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1206363'>材则不试，生则不年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206363_comment'></div>天耶人耶，孰知其然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206363_comment'></div>葬之者兄，铭之者子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206363_comment'></div>孰啬其存，而厚其死<span class='inlineComment2'>（《后山居士文集》卷一八。）</span>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206363_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1206363'>杭：此下原衍「州」字，据马刻本、库本及备要本删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1206363_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155226'>情亲有乖隔，江湖成阻脩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155226'>脱尘度翠密，徐行当寻幽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155226'>各有惜别怀，共此一日留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155226'>意合岂待约，酒尽不更求。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155226'>坐有黄冠师，未解逍遥游。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155226'>兴来我与共，醉罢君当休。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155226'>僧房火可亲，此乐行且谋。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155226'>万事自纠纷，高怀元一丘。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155226'></div><div /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年9月18日</a>　在开封，为楼异作《面壁庵记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一五。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>面壁庵记<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年9月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206343")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206343'>禅之初祖圆觉老师始自天竺来，居嵩高少林道场，盖面壁者九年，二祖禅师断臂立雪，世举知之，而昧其处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206343_comment'></div>自少林行殿而西，林篁阴郁，千步而近，度密越阻，群山四临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206343_comment'></div>前则少室诸峰嵱嵷连属，后则五乳崒兀拥掩，如举手内向，中峰之下，乃其故处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206343_comment'></div>有泉泠然，始至无水，以杖刺地，随举而涌，引而东出，世因号以锡杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206343_comment'></div>而丛榛族棘，荒秽翳塞，兔蹊雉域，蛇鼯所舍，樵牧避焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206343_comment'></div>元祐二年，留守简翼张公求而得之，始往过焉，使作亭以识其处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206343_comment'></div>除地得趾，层甓宛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206343_comment'></div>后十有馀年，知登封县楼君异复往过之，谓长老清江：「襄棘开道，使有人声马迹，再至则治矣，盍复其故」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206343_comment'></div>对曰：「下南山之木，出西谷之竹，伐薪以陶，率少而役，可立具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206343_comment'></div>其所乏者财尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206343_comment'></div>异请任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206343_comment'></div>于时众治泰陵，休于次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206343_comment'></div>异敬以请，自监司与百局之执事及郡县之令丞佐尉，下逮工贾士庶，不挽而同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206343_comment'></div>于是智者谋，仁者施，壮效其力，工献其伎，为堂为室，图像陈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206343_comment'></div>守卫有次，门庑有列，盖一朝而具，既月而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206343_comment'></div>而林出芝十有二本，华各异色，茎如漆饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206343_comment'></div>甘露雨于泉池，夜有光气四起属天，合为大练，东西数十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206343_comment'></div>呜呼，其兴可量也耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206343_comment'></div>夫道一，而今之教者三，三家之后相与诋訾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206343_comment'></div>盖世异则教异，教异则说异，尽己之道则人之道可尽，究其说则他说亦究，其相訾也固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206343_comment'></div>三圣之道非异，其传与不传也耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206343_comment'></div>子孔子之门，颜、闵、冉皆无传，仲弓之后则有荀卿，曾舆之后则有孟轲，端木赐之后则有庄休，而荀、孟、庄之后无传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206343_comment'></div>李氏之传关尹，尹之传复无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206343_comment'></div>释自能仁二十八世为初祖之东，六世为曹溪，曹溪至今又十有五世矣，而儒、老子之徒欲与校其原委，误矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206343_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206343_comment'></div>道之不传，盖始于此，历岁千百，逮今而兴，岂有待于异耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206343_comment'></div>建中靖国元年九月十八日，居士陈师道记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206343_comment'></div>比丘昙潜书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1206343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年11月23日</a>　预郊祀礼，感寒得疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年12月29日</a>　卒，虚岁五十，实岁四十九。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
安康（西城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d226ba362424440b827936201c5fd379_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d226ba362424440b827936201c5fd379");'><span id='d226ba362424440b827936201c5fd379_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1971')">1072-1971年</a>，21-卒后870年</div><div id='d226ba362424440b827936201c5fd379' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1971')">1072-1971年</a>　陈师道随父在金州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　陈师道随父在金州，为知州刘某作忘归亭记。作品：《忘归亭记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1206330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忘归亭记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206330")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206330'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206330'>熙宁七年，尚书水部郎中开封刘君刺守金州，政平岁丰，士民康乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206330_comment'></div>乃作亭于此城之上，以望牛山而临汉水，以乐府僚属、四方之游士，名之曰「忘归亭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206330_comment'></div>又使其客彭城陈师道记其意曰：西城治汉上游，庐舍弊陋，市肆落莫，名虽为州，实不如秦、楚下县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206330_comment'></div>山林四塞，行数百千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206330_comment'></div>水道阻险，转缘山间，悬流逆折，触石破舟，回洑平渊，深昧不测，射工、水蛭，中人多死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206330_comment'></div>陆行凭陵，因山梯石，悬栈过险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206330_comment'></div>修林丛竹，悍蛇鸷兽，卒出杀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206330_comment'></div>家有蛊厉，乘间行毒，邻里无过从，行路不敢饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206330_comment'></div>拥掩荫郁，日月隐蔽，夜长昼短，暄寒无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206330_comment'></div>又多雾雨，疾疢易作，土疏河润，地气发泄，多病脚弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206330_comment'></div>废丘故宫，颓城败冢，达于四境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206330_comment'></div>狐鸣鸟声，日夜间作，使人怅然怀归，凄然发叹，挥然出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206330_comment'></div>于是相与登斯亭以向坐，则又志意舒徐，气血和平，蘧然而笑，栩然而歌，超然而忘归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206330_comment'></div>其山川之美，临观之乐，不言可知，言不能尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206330_comment'></div>士大夫去坟墓，背田庐，捐宗姻友旧，从事于异域，故虽君子无厌苦之志而有归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206330_comment'></div>居官有守，义不得去，念岁月之永而忧不可极，作为斯亭，与人同乐，以居而忘怀，其志壮哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206330_comment'></div>公以治人，私以养生，古之政也，某敢不承君之命！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1206330_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

DetailSwitch("9523f14ab4ce4ed6a738c1fc315c401b");'><span id='9523f14ab4ce4ed6a738c1fc315c401b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: -----title
杭州（钱塘）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='97e02ce3bb33483e8a14b290744dd819_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("97e02ce3bb33483e8a14b290744dd819");'><span id='97e02ce3bb33483e8a14b290744dd819_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>，30岁</div><div id='97e02ce3bb33483e8a14b290744dd819' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年8月</a>　八月，陈师道至杭州。作品：《次韵寄答晁无咎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_155196' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155196' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155196?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵寄答晁无咎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155196")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155196_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155196'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155196'>西湖欲雨厨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>烟满，风叶倒囊云覆碗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155196'>望湖楼上白头人，独倚栏干谁肯伴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155196'>独有诗人记病身，清风千里寄行尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155196'>豪华信有回天力，惊开桃李闲新春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155196'>往事不回如过雨，醉梦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_155196", 155196, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>恍然</span>忘恶语<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155196'>人生如幻此何尤，未信黄金贵于土。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155196'>爱子千篇顷刻成，借将胸腹诧吴人。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155196'>吟哦怪有芳鲜气，却被湖山识姓名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155196'>文章废退知难强，身外<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_155196", 155196, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>虚华</span>本无望。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155196'>何曾临水惜芒鞋，却解逢人拈拄杖。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155196'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_155196", 155196, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>眼根</span>清净尘不留，登伽过尽不回头<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：来诗云不应越女三年留。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155196'>家在中原归未得，江淮断道无行舟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155196'>两山相逢翻手疾，欲谋一笑宁无日。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155196'>却惭怀朴似周人，祇可闻名不须识。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155196'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_155196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155196'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_155196_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本、张本作树</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_155196_0'>⑵ 自注：前在澶州，有读无咎文，编诗因以戏之。无咎今以为言。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_155196_0'>⑶ 自注：苏子瞻诗云游遍钱塘湖上境，归来文字带芳鲜。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155196_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州（江都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='68d13699bee24a4ca82681d07fab9d71_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("68d13699bee24a4ca82681d07fab9d71");'><span id='68d13699bee24a4ca82681d07fab9d71_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>，31岁</div><div id='68d13699bee24a4ca82681d07fab9d71' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　陈师道自杭州北归，途经扬州，遇秦观于逆旅，匆匆别去。<br /></div>

-----title
许昌（长社）
-----detail

-----title
巨野
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e6201444a35b462d85c4f32745e64cd7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6201444a35b462d85c4f32745e64cd7");'><span id='e6201444a35b462d85c4f32745e64cd7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>，39岁</div><div id='e6201444a35b462d85c4f32745e64cd7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>移颍州教授，冬日，自徐赴颍。作品：《巨野二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。自徐州移颍州，巨野恐非必经之地，然后来绍圣四年春自曹州归徐州途径巨野，时令又与此二诗中至秋景不合，姑从冒笺系于此年。）</span>《出清口》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷三、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。此诗具体写作背景不详，任渊《年谱》系于此年，从之，姑系于自徐赴颍途中。）</span><div id='poem_154642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154642")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154642'>红落芙蕖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>晚，青深蒲稗秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154642'>平湖无过鸟，鸣鼓有行舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_154642'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_154642_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本作蓉</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_154642_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_154641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154641?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154641'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154641'>蒲港侵衣绿，莲塘乱眼红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154641'>将身供世事，结缆待回风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154641'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154641_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>出清口</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155170")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155170'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155170'>家世山东饱耕稼，晚托一舟顺流下。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155170'>渔沟寒饼不下箸，推柂转头更五夜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155170'>平明放溜出清口，霜落潮回雾连野。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155170'>平淮一梦三十里，有日无风神所借。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155170'>似怜忧患满人间，百孔千疮容<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>一罅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155170'>文章<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_155170", 155170, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>末技</span>将自效，语不惊人神可吓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155170'>子女玉帛君所馀，寄声白鸟烦多谢。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155170'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_155170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155170'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_155170_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本作留</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155170_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f5f6f0b3b2f1438a8e400568d18c8df1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f5f6f0b3b2f1438a8e400568d18c8df1");'><span id='f5f6f0b3b2f1438a8e400568d18c8df1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>，46岁</div><div id='f5f6f0b3b2f1438a8e400568d18c8df1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　春，离曹州归徐州，过巨野。作品：《刘道原画像赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一七。）</span>《是是亭记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一五。）</span>《巨野》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷二。此诗任渊定为元祐二年作，冒笺定为得徐州教授还乡道中作，见冒笺53页，考《中国历史地图集》，自开封至徐州，巨野非必经之地，自曹州至徐州，由水道则正经巨野，故系于此年经巨野之时。）</span><div id='poem_1206349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘道原画像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206349")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206349'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206349'>是非贤否，一世所同，既久则反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206349_comment'></div>岂同时皆愚而后之人皆智？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206349_comment'></div>盖利害好恶出焉，则毁誉不得其正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206349_comment'></div>以是而言，则前私而后公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206349_comment'></div>汉之人谓公孙丞相为贤，汲黯为戆，至于今则公孙谀而汲直也，其相反盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206349_comment'></div>庐山刘道原，豪杰名节之士，黯之流者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206349_comment'></div>以义正利，以直正曲，危言特行，别析是非白黑，丝发不贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206349_comment'></div>如权衡量度，如水之鉴，如绳之度，既不可欺以私，又不得逃其目，虽一时贵权气炎势力排山倒海不置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206349_comment'></div>死生穷达，不到其心，故终其身亦不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206349_comment'></div>当道原之时，识与不识，相随诋之，如复仇施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206349_comment'></div>其逝未几，而念慕叹咏，恨其生之晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206349_comment'></div>更千百岁，日远一日，公则宜如何也耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206349_comment'></div>虽然，武帝奴视卫大将军、傲丞相而敬黯，淮南诸子其怨汉至不沐浴三十年，独畏黯不敢发，又为之寝谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206349_comment'></div>其君臣相谓丞相可说，大将军虽不可说盖可刺也，至黯复不敢刺，则其同时固有知之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206349_comment'></div>其所谓戆，以其不知利尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206349_comment'></div>利非黯所知也，丞相则知之矣，故可说而下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206349_comment'></div>道原遭时承平，故其效莫见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206349_comment'></div>虽然，小人之为不善，盖有畏而不发者矣，其补于世岂小哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206349_comment'></div>绍圣四年春过巨野，佐有羲仲者，其子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206349_comment'></div>始拜其像而叹曰：晋人有云，「廉、蔺虽千载，凛有生气，曹、李虽在，已如九泉下人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206349_comment'></div>士虽后之，其何恨！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206349_comment'></div>为之赞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1206349'>孰屈不伸，有亡有存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206349_comment'></div>有一其得，曷校后前！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206349_comment'></div>其刚斯何，宁折不靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206349_comment'></div>其直斯何，正人如己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206349_comment'></div>贤则过之，张而不弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206349_comment'></div>维利不嗜，不侮不畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206349_comment'></div>貌不踰中，气盖一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206349_comment'></div>维死不忌，子立特起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206349_comment'></div>黄、范、司马，既叙且铭，自足以达，况兹其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206349_comment'></div>千载之下，凛然其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206349_comment'></div>载之丹青，益永阙闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1206349_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>是是亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年2月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206340")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206340'>刘子佐巨野，筑室以居，名曰是是之亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206340_comment'></div>而语客曰：「吾刚不就俗，介不容众，而人亦不吾容也，故吾勉焉，是其所是而不非其所非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206340_comment'></div>又惧有时而忘之也，以名吾居，耳目属焉，亦盘盂、几杖、服佩之类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206340_comment'></div>吾其免乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206340_comment'></div>客笑之曰：「是是近谄，非非近讪，不幸而过，宁讪毋谄」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206340_comment'></div>以病刘子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206340_comment'></div>晁子闻而作，曰：「事无常是，亦无常非，使天下举以为非，而子独是之，何所取正？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206340_comment'></div>使天下举以为是，而子独非之，安得力而胜诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206340_comment'></div>尝与子问津于无可无不可之涂，而弭节乎两忘之圃，夫安知吾是之所在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206340_comment'></div>又为之赋以砭刘子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206340_comment'></div>陈子见而叹曰：「夫三子之言，其皆有所激乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206340_comment'></div>今夫是非参于前，子将称其所是而默其所非，自以为得矣，而曾不思默而不称，则固已非之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206340_comment'></div>使世皆愚则可以默而欺之，而世不皆愚也，其有知之者矣，吾惧子之不免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206340_comment'></div>夫是其所非则为谄，非其所是则为讪，是非不失其正，二何有焉，客之笑非子之病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206340_comment'></div>夫道二，理与事是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206340_comment'></div>是非两忘者理也，有是与非者事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206340_comment'></div>事待理而后立，理待事而后行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206340_comment'></div>今使刘子忘而不有，于事犹有阙乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206340_comment'></div>晁子之砭，非子之药也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206340_comment'></div>刘子名某，南康人，其大父凝之，有所不顾，举世挽之不能回也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206340_comment'></div>仕不合而去，老于庐山之下，庐陵文忠公为赋《庐山高》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206340_comment'></div>其父道原，面数人短长，不避权贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206340_comment'></div>群居聚语，是是非非，公无所隐，闻者至心掉手失，掩耳疾走，而略不以为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206340_comment'></div>卒穷以死，而天下归重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206340_comment'></div>今刘子博览伟辩，刻身苦思，既嗣其世而向善，雠恶亦不减其二父，而又能沈潜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1206340", 1206340, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>摧折</span>，以成其材，故士君子皆乐告以善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206340_comment'></div>孟子曰「是非之心，智之端也」，又曰「无是非之心，非人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206340_comment'></div>薋菉之不知，白黑之不分，固士之所弃，而尽言以招过，又昔人之所戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206340_comment'></div>然则何施而可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206340_comment'></div>夫明天下之是非者，智也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206340_comment'></div>正天下之是非者，任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206340_comment'></div>进则见于事，退则见于书，子姑明之，二者必有别矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206340_comment'></div>绍圣四年二月五日，彭城陈师道记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1206340_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154817?labeling=true' target='_blank'>巨野</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154817")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154817'><div class='poemSentence' -----title
淮安（山阳）

id='poem_sentence_3_155289'>志行万里困一误，吐豆龁荄甘伏枥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155289'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155289_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阜阳（汝阴）

id='poem_sentence_2_155181'>非公无此客，请寿两山樽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155181'>叔季大儒后，偏醒亦同醺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155181'>心与柏石坚，章成绮绣纹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155181'>多难独不补，少戆今无闻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155181'>时无古今异，智有功名昏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155181'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_155181_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年10月25日</a>　奉遣与苏迨同祷雨于张龙公祠，既得雨，十一月十日，复与苏迨同往送神。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_155275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155275'>道人赞公徒，相识几生前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155275'>子亦怜我老，我岂要子怜。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155275'>会逢万里风，一系五湖船。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155275'>酌我岩下水，咽子山中篇。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155275'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_155275_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　正月末，苏轼改知扬州，早春，欧阳棐离颍，师道同赵令畤赋诗送之，苏轼亦次韵。作品：《送叔弼寄秦张》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_155261' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155261' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155261?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送叔弼寄秦张</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155261")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155261_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155261'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155261'>庐陵四公子，吾及识其半。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155261'>叔也英达人，平易亦精悍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155261'>于时吾始壮，败壁不涂墁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155261'>孤身客东都，转食诸公馆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155261'>时来扣君门，百过<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>不留难。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155261'>倾心倒囊笈，燕语彻昏旦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155261'>磬折晚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>为亲，少得而多患。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155261'>相过汝颍上，岁月不胜难<span class='inlineComment2'>（赵本、四库本、张本作叹）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155261'>君才得公馀，十日而千万。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155261'>舌端悬日月，笔下来江汉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155261'>此行不寻常，谈者方一贯。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155261'>逸足宁小试，宝刀当立断。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155261'>用意不崎岖，欲得忘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>挟弹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155261'>卧念<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>平生亲，稍作春冰泮。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155261'>因声督张秦，书来不应缓。<div id='poem_sentence_14_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_155261'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_155261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155261'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_155261_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本作遍</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_155261_0'>⑵ 赵本、四库本、张本作挽</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_155261_0'>⑶ 赵本、四库本、张本作志</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_155261_0'>⑷ 赵本、四库本、张本作目今</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155261_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　陈师道在颍州教授任。作品：《北渚》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷三。）</span>《东阡》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_154646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北渚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154646")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154646'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154646'>南荡不可度，北渚风浪生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154646'>向来狐兔迹，已复蛟鼍鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154646'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年2月25日</a>　陈师道为宋仁宗墨宝作序。作品：《御书后序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一五。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御书后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年2月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206291")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206291'>人皆有所好，其上胜之，其次任之，其下蕴崇之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206291_comment'></div>惟至人无好，有所好者，同于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206291_comment'></div>神文圣武皇帝其好之与人同，其胜之与人异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206291_comment'></div>同以为德，异以为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206291_comment'></div>迩声色而欲不胜礼，宝珠玉而利不胜义，时游田而逸不胜度，故其在位四十馀年，而四方百物无所损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206291_comment'></div>顾好飞白书，明窗净几，时一为之，以侈其好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206291_comment'></div>于是将相宗戚，家有藏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206291_comment'></div>臣不知书，不能颂其美，而窃有所叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206291_comment'></div>凡艺不滞古则徇今，滞古则舍己而就规矩，徇今则略法而逐世好，故其弊，君臣争名，而祸乱从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206291_comment'></div>臣窃窥观皇帝会法而忘世，会理而忘法，故工拙偏正不足论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206291_comment'></div>所谓有其道而进于技者，王者之于艺盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206291_comment'></div>彭城王氏世为贵将，故其家有传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206291_comment'></div>其从孙万寿主簿臣有基以皇帝所书六大字以示臣，臣盖望而知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206291_comment'></div>臣不知书，然望而知之者，臣以理得之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206291_comment'></div>臣惟皇帝却天下之好而留神翰墨，乃帝者之懿德，来世之伟闻，而臣实惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206291_comment'></div>臣闻故老言当斯之时，二府百吏，内宗外姻，下逮近习，莫不好书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206291_comment'></div>夫士大夫阿主之好而为书，未害于政，而臣惧小人因书以进也，故君子于其所好又有慎焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206291_comment'></div>臣惟皇帝之知此，故世无其传，而臣之愚不得不惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206291_comment'></div>元祐七年二月二十五日，颍州教授臣陈师道谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206291_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ddf03df1f2b749ceb36815e85bd9bc3f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ddf03df1f2b749ceb36815e85bd9bc3f");'><span id='ddf03df1f2b749ceb36815e85bd9bc3f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1094')">1092-1094年</a>，41-43岁</div><div id='ddf03df1f2b749ceb36815e85bd9bc3f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　二月，晏知止知颍州，六月，韩川知颍州，陈师道等前往迎接韩川。作品：《迎新将至漕城》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_154688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎新将至漕城暮归遇雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154688")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154688'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154688'>早投林野违风雨，晚旁尘泥饱送迎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154688'>却愧两街屠贩子，卧听车马过桥声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154688'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　作诗送赵令畤离颍。作品：《送赵承议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_155007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155007?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送赵承议<span class='inlineComment2'>（令畤）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155007")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155007'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155007'>先生<span class='inlineComment2'>（高丽本作王）</span>隐德世难名，晚见诸孙也自成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155007'>颍水向来须好句，道山今日有宗英。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155007'>林湖更觉追随尽，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_155007", 155007, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>巾帽</span>犹堪语笑倾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155007'>勤苦读书终不补，未须墙角弃长檠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155007'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155007_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　为黄庭坚母李夫人作墓志铭。作品：《李夫人墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1206357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李夫人墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206357")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206357'>夫人建昌人，李姓，溧水尉、赠特进之子，大理丞、知康州黄庶之妻，集贤校理、佐著作庭坚之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206357_comment'></div>初，特进贤其子，不妄与人，久之以归康州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206357_comment'></div>康州佐大臣幕府，持议不挠，大臣外敬内怀，以故官不达，夫人安之以相焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206357_comment'></div>康州卒，子稚而贫，夫人以丧还葬豫章，遣子就学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206357_comment'></div>或劝以利，夫人曰：「自我家及儿父时，未尝不贫，何用利」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206357_comment'></div>其后校理仕于朝，名伟人，士倾下之，然亦以是数致言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206357_comment'></div>校理谢不谨，为夫人忧，夫人曰：「大者吾望汝，细何忧焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206357_comment'></div>夫人始封寿光，校理辞所拜官，进封安康郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206357_comment'></div>元祐六年，年七十二，卒于东都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206357_comment'></div>五男，大临、叔献、叔达、仲熊，校理其次也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206357_comment'></div>四女，有妇行，长为洪氏妇，其死不幸，校理是以赋《毁璧》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206357_comment'></div>于是大临为梁县尉，而仲熊卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206357_comment'></div>诸子名文行，而梁县法度之士也，世以是贤夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206357_comment'></div>明年，合于康州之墓，在分宁之台平，实双井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206357_comment'></div>梁县与其群弟使来言曰：「先实知子，子其铭以寿吾先」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206357_comment'></div>师道学于校理，贫不自食，又客焉，知其私为详，不辞而铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206357_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1206357'>妇患不德，不患不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206357_comment'></div>惟其身之，孰不承之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206357_comment'></div>特进之子，康州之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206357_comment'></div>善于其身，内外具宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206357_comment'></div>翁姑如亲，夫夫妇妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206357_comment'></div>盍监其子，则知其母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206357_comment'></div>孰吾孰汝，五子如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206357_comment'></div>敬而不忌，以有其室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206357_comment'></div>娣姒之间，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1206357", 1206357, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>庸庸</span>坦坦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206357_comment'></div>不愧以长，覆护其短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206357_comment'></div>内仁族姻，外事宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206357_comment'></div>哭有馀哀，室无遗帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206357_comment'></div>孰不贵富，以亡为存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206357_comment'></div>孰不老寿，以死为生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206357_comment'></div>死而不腐，何有于文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206357_comment'></div>我其矢之，以累斯人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1206357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　陈师道子陈登生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年6月15日</a>　为彭城县令作移狱记。作品：《彭城移狱记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>彭城移狱记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206335")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206335'>徐居东方，为南境梁、楚之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206335_comment'></div>其地四来，无林泽之阻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206335_comment'></div>其民<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1206335", 1206335, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>拙木</span>，无武击之技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206335_comment'></div>而其治多狱，其狱多盗，其盗多劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206335_comment'></div>论以重典，购以重赏，死者岁以百计，购以巨万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206335_comment'></div>余徐人也，知其说焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206335_comment'></div>庆历、嘉祐之间，曹、濮两州称为盗区，始用权制，而徐故无盗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206335_comment'></div>治平末，有为徐守，舍萧，盗夜穴其室，私其装焉，于是请用重法，而盗由是兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206335_comment'></div>古之为盗有三：惰民无生业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206335_comment'></div>恶子多费，取资于人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206335_comment'></div>凶年穷里老弱死闾巷，壮者起而自救，郡国亡命依阻深昧，以缓朝夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206335_comment'></div>今之为盗有二：两军亡卒无以自存，县之尉士终更罢归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206335_comment'></div>凡民去耒耜，更邑市，偷惰侈靡，不能自还，而其技足使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206335_comment'></div>重法之盗有二；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206335_comment'></div>奸猾诱民为盗而反告；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206335_comment'></div>逐捕之吏以窃为彊，上下相通，以掠服之，不然毒死狱中以幸赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206335_comment'></div>徐之盗有二：其愚易罔，其拙不能自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206335_comment'></div>凡为盗者五，而徐之为盗九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206335_comment'></div>凡盗不急利则缓死，而徐之盗以身为市而就死也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206335_comment'></div>凡盗抵法，而徐之盗罔于法也，可不察乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206335_comment'></div>夫刑之不胜盗久矣，故季康子以为患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206335_comment'></div>智之不胜盗久矣，故赵京兆盗谋辄觉，而不能禁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206335_comment'></div>购之不胜盗久矣，为购以尽敌也，盗可尽乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206335_comment'></div>然则胜之者可不可也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206335_comment'></div>刘叔贡父为曹州，盗贼衰息，狱屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206335_comment'></div>或问弭盗之术，叔贡父曰：「吾何术焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206335_comment'></div>不以重地视之而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206335_comment'></div>有为勾容令，多盗，改置社稷而加礼焉，既而盗止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206335_comment'></div>先君子所说、先吏所为，世必以为难，而今人所行、世所共知者，复何难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206335_comment'></div>盖世以簿书讼狱为治，故意不及其外而一切绝之，非行之难，而不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206335_comment'></div>此两人者，特一其所遇，敬其所事，而其效如此，又况古之人善其身而行之者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206335_comment'></div>彭城狱故近市，汶阳梁叔忱废县圃而徙之，为南北之室，以时寒暑，不以考掠，而狱益明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206335_comment'></div>叔忱为令有能声，方地数百，历年数十，未有其比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206335_comment'></div>余为徐学官，过之，见其兴作，而属余为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206335_comment'></div>会徙颍，不果作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206335_comment'></div>明年狱成，使来告而记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206335_comment'></div>后之人以余所称为心，以叔忱所治为法，彭城之狱庶其清乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206335_comment'></div>叔忱名子谅，丞相庄肃公之孙，以承议郎知县事云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206335_comment'></div>元祐七年六月十五日，陈师道记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1206335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年8月3日</a>　为甄氏思亭作记。作品：《思亭记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>思亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206334")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206334'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206334'>甄，故徐富家，至甄君始以明经教授，乡称善人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206334_comment'></div>而家益贫，更数十岁不克葬，乞贷邑里，葬其父母昆弟凡几丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206334_comment'></div>邑人怜之，多助之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206334_comment'></div>既葬，益树以木，作室其旁，而问名于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206334_comment'></div>余以谓目之所视而思从之，视干戈则思斗，视刀锯则思惧，视庙社则思敬，视第家则思安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206334_comment'></div>夫人存好恶喜惧之心，物至而思，固其理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206334_comment'></div>今夫升高以望松梓，下丘垄而行墟墓之间，棘荆莽然，狐兔之迹交道，其有不思其亲者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206334_comment'></div>请名之曰「思亭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206334_comment'></div>亲者，人所不忘也，而君子慎之，故为墓于郊而封沟之，为庙于家而尝禘之，为衰为忌而悲哀之，所以存其思也，其可忘乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206334_comment'></div>虽然，自亲而下至于服尽，服尽则情尽，情尽则忘之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206334_comment'></div>夫自吾之亲而至于忘之者，远故也，此亭之所以作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206334_comment'></div>凡君之子孙登斯亭者，其有忘乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206334_comment'></div>因其亲以广其思，其有不兴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206334_comment'></div>君曰：「博哉，子之言也，吾其庶乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206334_comment'></div>曰：「未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206334_comment'></div>贤不肖异思，后岂不有望其木思以为材，视其榛棘思以为薪，登其丘墓思发其所藏者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206334_comment'></div>于是遽然流涕以泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206334_comment'></div>曰：「未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206334_comment'></div>吾为子记之，使君之子孙诵斯文者，视其美以为劝，视其恶以为戒，其可免乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206334_comment'></div>君揽涕而谢曰：「免矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206334_comment'></div>遂为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206334_comment'></div>元祐七年八月三日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1206334_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年8月10日</a>　陈师道在颍州教授任。作品：《八月十日二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_154626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八月十日二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年8月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154626")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154626'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154626'>一梦人间四十年，只应炊灶固依然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154626'>两官不办一丘费，五字虚随万里船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154626'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154626_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154625' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154625?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年8月10日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154625'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154625'>人生七十今强半，老去光阴已后身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154625'>更欲置身须世外，世间元自不关人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154625'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154625_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年8月14日</a>　为彭城县令作石记。作品：《彭城县令题名记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。此文一名为《彭城县令石记》）</span><div id='poem_1206336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>彭城县令题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206336")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206336'>庆历初，西边弛兵，益修政事，谓吏之近民莫如令，始出王官行县事，以休其民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206336_comment'></div>盖自选人三考，用举者为令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206336_comment'></div>令三考，用举者为京官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206336_comment'></div>京官满三岁为朝官，盖士之选者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206336_comment'></div>以选士治剧县若相宜，然而犹有不合者，岂法使然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206336_comment'></div>徐为州，部五县，而四用选令，故为难治，而彭城其尤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206336_comment'></div>昔汉宣帝责成郡国守相，班班声迹可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206336_comment'></div>今选士为令，于古为加详，而吏治不尽如古，其故何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206336_comment'></div>盖汉承秦弊，网目疏阔，吏自为治，故易为功，而非王制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206336_comment'></div>今法令备具，上下维持，中才可以守，而智者常患不尽其用，故其治难，无赫赫之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206336_comment'></div>虽然，善其身，明其视听，使民有所恃而不冤，亦可谓良有司矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206336_comment'></div>司马迁、班固传循吏不列县令，岂以令非王官，不登简策，略而不书耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206336_comment'></div>今皆天子命吏，可不自勉，使史氏有述焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206336_comment'></div>令厅故无记，承议郎梁君始追纪其名氏列于石，凡十九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206336_comment'></div>记与不记，不足为吏能否，而梁君力能及之，为有馀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206336_comment'></div>元祐七年八月十四日，陈师道记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206336_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1206336'>「元祐」句：原无，据马刻本、库本及备要本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1206336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1206336'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_1206336_0'>⑴ 《后山居士文集》卷一四。又见《古今合璧事类备要》卷七九，《古今事文类聚》外集卷一四，道光《铜山县志》卷一八。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1206336_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/154679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>即事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_4_154991_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154990?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154990'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154990'>经史三年学，聪明一旦开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
