id='poem_sentence_4_154990'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在颍州教授任，夏末，罢官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6f59cd0402334f18bafc80b53ff5e3e4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6f59cd0402334f18bafc80b53ff5e3e4");'><span id='6f59cd0402334f18bafc80b53ff5e3e4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，43岁</div><div id='6f59cd0402334f18bafc80b53ff5e3e4' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋冬之际归颍州摒挡行李，为比丘理公作塔铭。作品：《比丘理公塔铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1206367' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206367' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206367?labeling=true' target='_blank'>比丘理公塔铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206367")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206367_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206367'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206367'>绍圣元年九月癸丑，比丘理公卒于汝阴之荐福院，年八十一，腊四十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206367_comment'></div>戊午，葬于西郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206367_comment'></div>始余为府属，闻其声，数过之，与语敬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206367_comment'></div>其后去官如东都，往问其疾且别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206367_comment'></div>于是疾久矣，貌言如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206367_comment'></div>既别，且曰：「公老而疾，有如尽缘，我其铭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206367_comment'></div>公嘿然，归则葬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206367_comment'></div>其属永圆既治其丧，又具石以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206367_comment'></div>公名悟理，赵郡袁氏子也，去家居东都宝安院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206367_comment'></div>持律严密，遍习相性圆教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206367_comment'></div>始出汝阴，證悟禅师在焉，闻其道，辍讲谢徒而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206367_comment'></div>證悟敬焉，使如瑞光，又事圆照禅师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206367_comment'></div>久而还居荐福，日诵《金刚》、《行愿》两经，阖户禅观，不近人事凡二十年，颍人向焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206367_comment'></div>晚谓禅者普仁曰：「明年吾往矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206367_comment'></div>既疾，又谓永圆曰：「九月十八日，吾其已乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206367_comment'></div>实以既望坐逝，后三日而用火，盖先期焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206367_comment'></div>使以所诵经与所著书从葬，问故，曰：「葬有塔，诸天致敬，我不足当也，得此则免矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206367_comment'></div>既化，舍利五色，骨如积雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206367_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1206367'>理公<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1206367", 1206367, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>詻詻</span>，既平以直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206367_comment'></div>且学且弃，以究其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206367_comment'></div>下席散徒，行其所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206367_comment'></div>阖门谢事，二十其年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206367_comment'></div>两林孤图，过者敬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206367_comment'></div>有经有传，以及我师。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1206367_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作诗送伯兄师黯赴吏部改官。作品：《送伯兄赴吏部改官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四。此诗具体所作时地不详，姑系于颍州未罢官时。）</span><div id='poem_154985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_154882'>离<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>合应生理，过逢岂近缘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154882'>情亲见今日，语妙记当年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154882'>闭户安禅主，冲风逆水船。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154882'>不应清夜月，故作别时圆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154882'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_154882'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_154882_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本作会</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_154882_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_155043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>离颍</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155043")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155043'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155043'>河市<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_155043", 155043, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>千人聚</span>，寒江百丈牵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155043'>吾生能几日，此地费三年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155043'>丛竹防供爨，池鱼已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_155043", 155043, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>割鲜</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155043'>拙勤终不补，他日愧无传。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155043'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155043_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155118?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155118")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155118_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155118'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155118'>湖上难为别，梅梢已著春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155118'>林喧乌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>啄啄，风过水鳞鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155118'>缘有三年尽，情无一日亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155118'>白头厌奔走，何地与为邻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155118'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155118'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_155118_0'>⑴ 高丽本、赵本、四库本、库注本作鸟</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155118_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_155208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155208?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舟中二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155208")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155208'>恶风横江江卷浪，黄流湍猛风用壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155208'>疾如万骑千里来，气压三江五湖上。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155208'>岸上<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_155208", 155208, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>空荒</span>火夜明，舟中起坐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>待残更。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155208'>少年行路今头白，不尽还家去国情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155208'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155208'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_155208_0'>⑴ 高丽本、四库本、库注本作坐起</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155208_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_155207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155207?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155207'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155207'>野火烧原雉昏雊，黄尘涨天牛乱斗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155207'>江间无日不风波，老去何时脱奔走。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155207'>诗书满腹不及口，遮日宁须钓竿手。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155207'>愧尔茅檐炙背人，仰目青天搔白首。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155207'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155207_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155236' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155236' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>规禅停云斋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155236")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155236_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155236'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155236'>净居众天人，宫殿随所适。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155236'>少仕老不归，重门闭榛棘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155236'>道人秀丛林，妙语出禅寂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155236'>是身如浮云，随处同建立。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155236'>平生与二子，嗜好用一律。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155236'>我此复助缘，语绮已多责。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155236'>何年一把茅，据坐孤崒嵂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155236'>呵佛骂祖师，涂糊千五百。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155236'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_155236_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为魏汶父作墓铭。作品：《魏嘉州墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。此文具体所作时地不详，文中言墓主死于绍圣元年二月己未，“明年二月甲子从葬寿春”，且有“汶来余于颍水之上以请，晁与余久，又与俱来，其何辞”之语，推测写作地点为颍州，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1206358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>魏嘉州墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣二年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206358")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206358'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206358'>魏氏望钜鹿，自汉兖州刺史衡之曾孙始居魏之馆陶，五世而至郑公，辩毅慈明，为唐宗臣，馆陶之魏始大，甲于国谱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206358_comment'></div>又五世而至司徒谟，谟之子别居歙之婺源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206358_comment'></div>其后四世而至尚书礼部侍郎讳羽，为太宗、真宗三司使十有八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206358_comment'></div>而生龙图阁直学士讳瓘，见微致大，功昭南邦，以吏部侍郎归老下蔡，葬寿春八公山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206358_comment'></div>仍父子赠太尉，在名臣之数，别为下蔡之魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206358_comment'></div>太尉两娶刁氏，有子十一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206358_comment'></div>君其第十子也，讳绍，字承之，任为将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206358_comment'></div>尝知虞城县，禁蒱博而盗止，留守下其法焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206358_comment'></div>勾当合流镇，岁大饥，君叹曰：「朝请而夕报亦不及矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206358_comment'></div>振廪，出以下估而后闻，旁近赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206358_comment'></div>通判绛州，行州事，新庙学，具师徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206358_comment'></div>士故沉浮俗间，檄县谕出之，讲试以时，君与其属过焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206358_comment'></div>后以右朝散郎知嘉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206358_comment'></div>自唐开元献荔子，而今乐用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1206358", 1206358, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>朱桑</span>，人始病之，久而微矣，不给其求而刑者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206358_comment'></div>嘉祐中，有良守哀之，作二诗刻石以讽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206358_comment'></div>君将行，要贵多求者，既至，摹其石诗以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206358_comment'></div>黠贾夺人盐井，更数守讼不决，君刑而还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206358_comment'></div>君孝友慎和，而不受私，居无子弟过，出有吏能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206358_comment'></div>常有劳，再登格，而赏不及，君亦不自言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206358_comment'></div>绍圣元年二月己未卒，年五十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206358_comment'></div>明年二月甲子，从葬寿春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206358_comment'></div>两母并封崇、荣二国夫人，而所生何氏别封旌德县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206358_comment'></div>娶李氏，左金吾卫大将军忠吉之女，封寿安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206358_comment'></div>三子：男汶，女嫁蔡州助教刁宝臣、濠州参军晁载之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206358_comment'></div>将葬，君夫人曰葬有铭，君之行治不可不书也，使晁载之具其事，曰：君常调不及用，循职而已，毋异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206358_comment'></div>既具，合宗而谋曰：「其谁铭」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206358_comment'></div>晁妇曰：「其陈氏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206358_comment'></div>不则没吾父矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206358_comment'></div>晁载之曰：「士求铭于陈氏，辞者屡矣，吾所见也，求可冀乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206358_comment'></div>其妇曰：「盍索其词以固请乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206358_comment'></div>于是汶来，及余于颍水之上以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206358_comment'></div>晁与余交，又与俱来，其何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206358_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1206358'>魏氏再显，惟其有继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206358_comment'></div>有作有承，以有其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206358_comment'></div>再登公师，有子之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206358_comment'></div>君伏不兴，亦保其世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206358_comment'></div>犍为之政，不侮不畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206358_comment'></div>更四十年，良有其二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206358_comment'></div>事惟其常，亦何以异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206358_comment'></div>夫人之云，铭则不愧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1206358_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

项城

-----title
东阿
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ee41a505b96d4d939996a24d0b9c453e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ee41a505b96d4d939996a24d0b9c453e");'><span id='ee41a505b96d4d939996a24d0b9c453e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>，44岁</div><div id='ee41a505b96d4d939996a24d0b9c453e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年3月29日</a>　三月，奉母携眷往岳父郭槩河北东路提刑任所，是月二十九日，行至东阿，母夫人病卒舟中，年七十七。<br /></div>

-----title
曹县（济阴）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='680209cb8c45498ab42cb873f8f83058_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("680209cb8c45498ab42cb873f8f83058");'><span id='680209cb8c45498ab42cb873f8f83058_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　秋冬间，岳父郭槩自澶州移知曹州，陈师道携眷往依之，居曹州，常与晁将之唱和。作品：《次韵答晁无斁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。据诗句“诗来霜雪后，更觉天宇净”，诗当作于冬日，任渊《年谱》系于绍圣二年乙亥。）</span>《次韵无斁偶作二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。据冒笺此诗作于绍圣乙亥，故系于此。）</span><div id='poem_155201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵答晁无斁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155201")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155201'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155201'>女生愿有家，名妾以不聘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155201'>田里亦慕君，又恶不由正。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155201'>欲行不问涂，已破宁顾甑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155201'>耕蚕无一廛，庖井要三径。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155201'>还家忧患馀，挽须儿女竞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155201'>十年宁有此，一寒可无命。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155201'>平生晁夫子，得士公室庆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155201'>稍无车马音，复作宾客请。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155201'>论文到韩李，念旧说苏郑。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155201'>长年断消息，独语谁和应。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155201'>此生恩未报，他日目不瞑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155201'>归卧无好怀，扣门有佳听。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155201'>诗来雪霜<span class='inlineComment2'>（各本作霜雪）</span>后，更觉天宇净。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155201'>少好老未工，持刃授子柄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154845'>已传乌鹊喜，欲听鹡鸰声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154845'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154845_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154844?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_155172'>巧作松身与镜面，借美于外非良质。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155172'>潘翁拜跪摩老眼，一生再见三叹息。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155172'>了知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_155172", 155172, id='poem_sentence_4_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155172'>黄金白璧孰不有，古锦句囊聊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>可敌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155172'>睿思殿里春夜半，灯火阑残歌舞散。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155172'>自书细字答边臣，万里风尘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>入长算。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155172'>初闻桥山送弓剑，宁知玉碗人间见。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155172'>夜光炎炎冲斗牛，会有太史占星变。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155172'>人生尤物不必有，时一过目惊老丑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155172'>念子何忍遽磨研，少待须臾图不朽<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155172'>明窗净几风日暖，有愁万斛才八斗。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155172'>径须脱帽<span class='link' 赵本、四库本作那</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_155172_0'>⑵ 《玉海》三四《元祐神宗御笔》引作烟</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_155172_0'>⑶ 魏衍注：少游之墨尝许先生为他日墓志润笔，先生尝语衍，作此时，少游尚无恙，然终先逝去。衍谨书。（注原缺，据各本补）</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155172_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_155303'>匿形注目摇两股，卒然一击势莫御。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155303'>十中失一八九取，吻间流血腹如鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155303'>却行奋臂吾甚武，明日淮南作端午。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155303'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155303_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_154741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154741?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陶朱公庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154741")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154741_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154741'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154741'>千篇奏牍漫多知，百战收功未出奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154741'>名下难居身可辱，却将湖海换西施。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154741'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154741_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　居曹州，常与晁将之唱和。作品：《次韵晁无斁夏雨》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。）</span>《寄无斁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_155195' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155195' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155195?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵晁无斁夏雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155195")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155195_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155195'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155195'>咫尺隔山海，作书问如何。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155195'>蚁垤既畜粮，蛙窟如鸣鼍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155195'>积暑复一雨，斧斫仍手摩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155195'>钩窗欲悬麻，出门已横河。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155195'>人言月离毕，未必致滂沱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155195'>东皋繁草木，兰艾不同科。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155195'>惊鱼畏密罟，独鸟鸣南柯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155195'>稍无虫飞喧，复觉蝉语多。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155195'>因声作好恶，与物殊未和。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155195'>卧闻夜来雨，归种故山禾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155195'>百年须下泽，万里付长罗。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155195'>先生断百好，尚以诗作魔。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155195'>缩子万言手，听渠七字哦。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155195'>室迩人则远，燕默劳者歌。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155195'>思君得老瘦，触热生积痾。<div id='poem_sentence_14_155195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_155195'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_155195_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155054' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155054' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155054?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄无斁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155054")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155054_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155054'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155054'>敬问晁夫子，官池几许深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155054_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155054'>已应飞鸟下，复作卧龙吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155054_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155054'>待我中痾愈，同君把臂临。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155054_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155054'>泥涂无去马，夏木有<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>来禽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155054_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155054'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155054_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155054'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_155054_0'>⑴ 赵本、四库本、张本作自</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155054_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　居曹州。作品：《次韵别张芸叟》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷八、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_154657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵别张芸叟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154657")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_154657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154657'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154657'>中年为别更堪频，四海无家托一身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154657'>此别时须问生死，孰知诗力解穷人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154657'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_154657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年8月10日</a>　居曹州，与开元寺主僧重宝往来。作品：《佛指记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1206338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>佛指记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年8月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206338")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206338'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206338'>建隆几年，皇师伐蜀，曹卒有在行者，樵刍山间，数见光气，发地得石函，藏佛指焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206338_comment'></div>念无所置，且畏夺，乃破臂而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206338_comment'></div>老而归兵，乞丐道路，开元寺法华院僧闻而收之，厚其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1206338", 1206338, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>供御</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206338_comment'></div>数岁，破臂出以报焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206338_comment'></div>后归上生，而僧持去，客成武，邑人迎供，得舍利无数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206338_comment'></div>上生主者重宝通三论，严律居众，供施不倦，思有以还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206338_comment'></div>会僧如东都，过曹，宝谕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206338_comment'></div>他日赴供西里，渡浰水，遇而申之，且厚其报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206338_comment'></div>僧行不辍，宝反随之，及郭，会僧市盗马，其主见而讼之，乃留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206338_comment'></div>宝请于州而得焉，骨裂苍然而无感应，疑为僧所欺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206338_comment'></div>余迎致兴国院，率私属而敬焉，供茶三盏，澄聚为华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206338_comment'></div>余谓宝曰：「非耶，何以致此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206338_comment'></div>其体坏色变，殆为物所触耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206338_comment'></div>如来铁钵，祖师所传、曹溪所藏者，南汉之霸迎入宫中，传之妇人，应手而裂，其何疑焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206338_comment'></div>宝曰：「我以水玉匣而藏之，使目可视而手不近，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206338_comment'></div>余应曰：「可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206338_comment'></div>退求于家，无物可施，为记其事，使疑者信，谤者悔，富者施，是亦一助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206338_comment'></div>语有之，欲知前时视今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206338_comment'></div>余以词义名次四君，而贫于一代，岂昔亦以文施耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206338_comment'></div>昔童子聚沙以戏，见佛而施，佛为授记，为转轮王福四之一，其后百年阿育王是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206338_comment'></div>转轮四王相好同佛，而王肤如错，人不可近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206338_comment'></div>施之人胜，故其报重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206338_comment'></div>施之物微，故其报轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206338_comment'></div>夫三界惟心，万法惟识，无待于事，而此何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206338_comment'></div>盖等心而施，则生与佛等，沙与金等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206338_comment'></div>事夺于理，故报随于理，心有分别，则物有高下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206338_comment'></div>理夺于事，故报从于事，岂不惟心也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206338_comment'></div>夫轮王大福也，特一念尔，顾其心之何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206338_comment'></div>我以文施，岂不可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206338_comment'></div>虽然，佛之报身，严以万德，穷其所以，必各有因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206338_comment'></div>是以菩萨虽證道体而具万行，盖未有无理之事、无事之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206338_comment'></div>则以文施，其有阙乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206338_comment'></div>客有言曰：「曹近京师，一有传焉，国将宝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206338_comment'></div>覆且不保，张之可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206338_comment'></div>余应之曰：「不然，佛无去来，而人有因缘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206338_comment'></div>因有厚薄，故缘有时限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206338_comment'></div>缘之所在，孰得止之，前日是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206338_comment'></div>以悲为心，明扬劝厉，与众兴福，则先佛之愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206338_comment'></div>若欲独善而私有之，虽缘于佛，其非贪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206338_comment'></div>行不契圣，鬼将夺之，不待缘也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206338_comment'></div>宝以为然，又曰：「我初出家，抽架上书，得《證道歌》，先能成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206338_comment'></div>虽听相论而喜性宗，暇则读之，我岂与有缘乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206338_comment'></div>三岁之后，将参学于东南而终老焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206338_comment'></div>余叹曰：「赵州、临济，皆曹人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206338_comment'></div>今数百岁矣，嗣古导今，将在子与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206338_comment'></div>夫人命呼吸间，三岁不亦远乎，与其悔后，宁好先耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206338_comment'></div>子与时竞，时不待子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206338_comment'></div>绍圣三年八月十日，居士陈师道记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1206338_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='604e86ba19ef41eb9945d972dac5f488_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("604e86ba19ef41eb9945d972dac5f488");'><span id='604e86ba19ef41eb9945d972dac5f488_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1097')">1096-1097年</a>，45-46岁</div><div id='604e86ba19ef41eb9945d972dac5f488' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年4月13日</a>　陈师道居曹州，为窦少府作诗序。作品：《书窦少府诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷九。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书窦少府诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年4月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206298")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206298'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206298'>窦君与先大夫游，以行义闻里中，而人不知其工于诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206298_comment'></div>其殁二十馀年而诗始传，以其有子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206298_comment'></div>善夫，君不亡矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206298_comment'></div>绍圣三年四月十三日，彭城陈师道书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年8月25日</a>　陈师道居曹州，为汳水新渠作记。作品：《汳水新渠记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一四。此文郑谱未系年，然时间清楚易补。）</span><div id='poem_1206337' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206337' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206337?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汳水新渠记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年8月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206337")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206337_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206337'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206337'>汳句于萧，其阙如玦，《水经》谓河至荥阳，莨荡渠出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206337_comment'></div>渠至阳武，其下为汝蔡水是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206337_comment'></div>其出为阴沟，沟至浚仪，其下为涡，别为汳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206337_comment'></div>汳至蒙别为获，馀波迤于淮阳，东历萧、彭城，入于泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206337_comment'></div>《注》谓鸿沟、官度、甾获、丹、浚，与渠一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206337_comment'></div>禹塞荥泽而通渠于甫田，其后河绝，旃然入焉，即索水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206337_comment'></div>《汉书·地理志》荥阳既有卞水，又有狼汤，而受泲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206337_comment'></div>蒙有获水，首受甾获，至彭城入泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206337_comment'></div>以余考之，《河渠书》云自禹之后，荥阳引河为鸿沟，以通宋、郑、陈、蔡、曹、卫，与济、汝、淮、泗会于楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206337_comment'></div>而《竹书纪年》梁惠成王入河于甫田，又引而东，明非禹之旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206337_comment'></div>《书》曰济入于河，东出于陶丘北者，入而复出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206337_comment'></div>溢为荥者，济之别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206337_comment'></div>荥波既猪者，障而东之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206337_comment'></div>《周官》又谓豫之川荥、洛，幽兖之川河、泲，则河南无济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206337_comment'></div>其谓莨荡受济，禹塞荥泽而用河者，皆失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206337_comment'></div>《汉志》莨荡无出，甾获无始，盖略之也，余谓与《经》合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206337_comment'></div>而荥水，诸书皆不载，又疑渠、汳为二，而荥有一焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206337_comment'></div>杜佑以《经》作于顺帝之后，诡诞无据，而《注》叙渠源，或河或泲，或河泲合，其说不一，次其所经，纷错悖戾，而《志》亦阔略，不具卞始末，盖皆不可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206337_comment'></div>自汉末河入于汳，灌注兖、豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206337_comment'></div>永平中导汳，自荥阳别而东北，至千乘入于海，而河于是故渎在新渠之南，《注》所谓绝河而受索自此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206337_comment'></div>隋开皇中，因汉之旧，导河于汳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206337_comment'></div>大业初，合河、索为通济渠，别而东南入于淮，而故道竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206337_comment'></div>今始东都受退水为臭河，于畿为白沟，于宋为沙，于单为石梁，于徐为汳，而入于南清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206337_comment'></div>南清，故泗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206337_comment'></div>盖自三都而东，畿、宋、亳、宿、单、济之间，千里四来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206337_comment'></div>而故道浅狭，春夏不胜舟，秋水大至，亦不能受也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206337_comment'></div>萧故附庸之国，城小不足居民，又列肆于河外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206337_comment'></div>每水至，南里之民皆徙避之，庐舍没焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206337_comment'></div>率数岁一逢，民以为病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206337_comment'></div>绍圣三年，县令朝奉郎张惇始自西河，因故作新，支为大渠，合于东河，以导滞而缓溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206337_comment'></div>于是富者出财，壮者出力，日劝旬劳，既月而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206337_comment'></div>邑人相与语曰：「渠议旧矣，更数令不决，而卒成于吾侯，孰有惠而不报者乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206337_comment'></div>于是不谋而同，欲纪于石，以属余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206337_comment'></div>余谓张侯其居善守，行峻而言通，以成其名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206337_comment'></div>以仕善义，不畏不侮，以登于治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206337_comment'></div>其可纪者多矣，而诸父兄弟独有见于末者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206337_comment'></div>夫善为治者，人知其善而已，至其所善，盖莫得而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206337_comment'></div>渠之兴作有迹，其效在今，此邑人之所欲书也，遂为之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206337_comment'></div>八月二十五日，彭城陈师道记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1206337'></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1206337_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　居曹州，常与晁将之唱和。作品：《次韵晁无斁冬夜见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷六、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。）</span>《寒夜有怀晁无斁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷一、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_154861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_154861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/154861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵晁无斁冬夜见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_154861")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_154861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_154861'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_154861'>寒窗冷砚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>欲生尘，短枕长衾却自亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_154861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_154861'>老子形骸从薄暮，先生意气尚青春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_154861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154861'>覆杯不待回<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_154861", 154861, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>丹颊</span>，危坐犹能作直身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_154861'>城郭山林两无得，暮年当复几沾巾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_154861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154861'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_154861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_154861'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_154861_0'>⑴ 高丽本、库注本作夜</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_154861_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_155287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒夜有怀晁无斁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155287")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155287'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155287'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_155287", 155287, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>同好</span>共城郭，十日不一顾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155287'>人事虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_155287", 155287, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>好乖</span>，吾生亦多忤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155287'>阖门对妻子，岁月不可度。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155287'>闭目宁用遮，停杯仍下箸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155287'>独无区中缘，永怀岩下趣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155287'>平生三径资，安得一朝具。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155287'>万里初<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_155287", 155287, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>历块</span>，前驱告曛暮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155287'>怀归属有思，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_155287", 155287, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>弃世</span>不待怒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155287'>老境厌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_155287", 155287, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>逶迟</span>，人情费将护。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155287'>向来张长公，吾亦从兹去。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155287'>灯花频作喜，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_155287", 155287, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>月色</span>正可步。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155287'>预恐何水曹，明朝有新句。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155287'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_155287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　居曹州。作品：《除夜》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷四、《后山诗注补笺》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_155030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155030")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155030'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155030'>七十已强半，所馀能几何。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155030'>悬知暮景促，更觉后生多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155030'>遁世名为累，留年睡作魔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155030'>西归端著便，老子不婆娑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155030_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155030'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155030_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年10月</a>　为魏衍父作墓铭。作品：《朝奉郎魏君墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一八。此文写作具体时间不详，然文中称墓主于绍圣三年十月十七日葬，故系于此年。）</span><div id='poem_1206359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉郎魏君墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206359")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206359'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206359'>朝奉魏君讳涛，字信卿，其先自魏徙徐，为彭城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206359_comment'></div>父吉，赠宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206359_comment'></div>母王氏，寿安县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206359_comment'></div>元祐二年四月六日卒于家，年五十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206359_comment'></div>娶刘氏，昌乐县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206359_comment'></div>有子曰衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206359_comment'></div>绍圣三年十月十七日，葬于白鹤乡立德里之故茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206359_comment'></div>衍有文行，力贫以葬曾妣而下八丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206359_comment'></div>乡里既共其事，而师道又考次君之志行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1206359", 1206359, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>张施</span>，而石铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206359_comment'></div>君始以进士为濮州参军，贾以赂冒官族，脱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1206359", 1206359, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>市版</span>，州下其事，君不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206359_comment'></div>其为河东从事，佐经略使刘庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206359_comment'></div>契丹与河东争界，而廷议欲割畀之，遣使临议，庠以属君，使不能屈则临以威，君不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206359_comment'></div>于是复宪州，筑惠宁、肃定、神木三堡，声势益张，契丹亦不竞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206359_comment'></div>庠由是益知之，谓可当大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206359_comment'></div>士有罪当赎，而后使欲刑，君独不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206359_comment'></div>使武吏叫怒，僚吏却愕，君又独曰：「希意<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1206359", 1206359, "Clauses/45/Comments/1")'>顺事</span>，为自计耳，于公何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206359_comment'></div>况又非某之所能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206359_comment'></div>使虽不喜而竟屈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206359_comment'></div>其知承县，两仇斗而伤，决遣而伤者死，仇不自冤，而君疑之，求其故而未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206359_comment'></div>死者之子诉于监司，怒有恶语，君叹曰：「官可夺，囚不可杀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206359_comment'></div>不为具狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206359_comment'></div>后得其实，是夕罢归，醉骑及门，坠乃死，验其邻果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206359_comment'></div>其治明毅，所至不冤，而承人思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206359_comment'></div>至今衍常至其县，一县之人喜相告曰：「吾著作之子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206359_comment'></div>著作，君故官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206359_comment'></div>其监团柏镇，军兴，运夫过其郭，突门劫库兵，君出告曰：「尔去家度塞，父母妻子数日待还，今虽挟利器，怀重宝，何所归乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206359_comment'></div>众谕稍去，遂定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206359_comment'></div>君生十年丧父，哭之过哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206359_comment'></div>十八试礼部，闻母疾而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206359_comment'></div>其孝盖天资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206359_comment'></div>家产万金委群弟，不问所在，亡后争分，君又多予之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206359_comment'></div>有难之者，君不答，召衍而指其书，曰：「读此不患贫矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206359_comment'></div>君以不欺为心，亦不以告人，问其说，曰：「不自欺耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206359_comment'></div>而人信之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206359_comment'></div>外属为徐，守见而贤之，数荐宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206359_comment'></div>将用矣，君辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206359_comment'></div>或问之，曰：「班固以事窦氏为后所笑，可使后人笑我耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206359_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1206359'>魏氏隐微，及君而兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206359_comment'></div>得不偿出，亦古之曾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206359_comment'></div>凡君之行，出于不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206359_comment'></div>邑人之传，我则著之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1206359_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　居曹州。作品：《寄邓州杜侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷三、《后山诗注补笺》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_155271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄邓州杜侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155271")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_155271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155271'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155271'>南阳老幼如云屯，连日城东候使君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155271'>后者排前旁捷出，争先见面作慇勤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155271'>六年重来已白发，一日再见回青春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155271'>道傍过者怪相问，共言杜母真吾亲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155271'>使君虽老心尚壮，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_155271", 155271, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>文采风流</span>诸谢上。<div id='poem_sentence_4_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_155271'>名家从昔杜陵人，盛德于今丈人行。<div id='poem_sentence_5_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_155271'>我昔卧病老彭城，画船鸣鼓千里行。<div id='poem_sentence_6_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_155271'>致书馈奠初未识，丁宁劳苦如平生。<div id='poem_sentence_7_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_155271'>人言此事今未有，古人中求还得否。<div id='poem_sentence_8_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_155271'>忘年屈势不虚辱，公自<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>为德吾何取。<div id='poem_sentence_9_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_155271'>菊潭之水甘且洁，潭上秋花照山白。<div id='poem_sentence_10_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_155271'>请公酌此寿百年，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_155271", 155271, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>奕奕</span>长为此邦伯。<div id='poem_sentence_11_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_155271'>孰先一州后四方，重金叠盖登庙堂。<div id='poem_sentence_12_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_155271'>请从今日至云来，月三十斛输洛阳。<div id='poem_sentence_13_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_155271'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_155271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_155271'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_155271_0'>⑴ 高丽本、库注本作取，任渊校：一作自</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_155271_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: -----title
泰安（奉符）

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　七月，除棣州教授，其冬赴任。作品：《宿柴城》<span 商河

id='poem_sentence_1_154901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_154901'>客久艰难极，情忘去就轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_154901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_154901_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206299' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206299' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206299?labeling=true' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206299'>晁无咎云，眉山公之词盖不更此境也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206299_comment'></div>余谓不然，宋玉初不识巫山神女而能赋之，岂待更而知也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206299_comment'></div>余他文未能及人，独于词自谓不减秦七、黄九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206299_comment'></div>而为乡掾三年，去而复还又三年矣，而乡妓无欲余之词者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206299_comment'></div>独杜氏子勤恳不已，且云所得诗词满箧，家多畜纸笔墨，有暇则学书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206299_comment'></div>使不如言，其志亦可喜也，乃写以遗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206299_comment'></div>古语所谓「但解闭门留我处，主人莫问是谁家」者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206299_comment'></div>元符三年十一月一日，后山居士陈师道书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206299_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　十一月，改除秘书省正字，自赴棣州途中折返。作品：《除官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷五、《后山诗注补笺》卷一二。）</span>《谢正字启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《后山居士文集》卷一三。）</span>《题王平甫帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《后山集》卷七、《后山诗注补笺》卷一二。此诗具体写作时间不详，姑从任渊《年谱》系于此。）</span><div id='poem_155268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155268?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除官<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155268")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155268_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_155268_0'>① 除正字（宋注本、高丽本、库注本、张本作十一月除秘书省正字）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155268'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155268'>扶老趋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_155268", 155268, id='poem_sentence_1_155268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155268'>肯著金根谬，宁辞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_155268", 155268, id='poem_sentence_3_155268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155268'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155268_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢正字启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_1206285")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206285'>帝者居尊举要，因任以责成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206285_comment'></div>为官择人，作新以续故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206285_comment'></div>必须养之有素，然后求之非艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206285_comment'></div>恭惟祖宗之远猷，创为馆阁之清选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206285_comment'></div>由二府之公举，开数路以博收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206285_comment'></div>不为常员，务在多得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206285_comment'></div>给太官之上膳，假四部之异书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206285_comment'></div>加以其年，孰不为用！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206285_comment'></div>凡百年名世之士，莫不由是以兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206285_comment'></div>而一代致平之功，其原盖出于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206285_comment'></div>名虽文学之选，实为将相之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206285_comment'></div>尤难其人，可称此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206285_comment'></div>如某材非适用，实不迨名，徒以生逢文武之兴，夙被父师之训，粗于翰墨，小有专勤，误蒙哲匠之评，堕在胜流之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206285_comment'></div>每深惟于弱质，久自绝于仕涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206285_comment'></div>本愿下乡，殁有善人之号；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206285_comment'></div>岂期莫齿，名玷荐贤之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206285_comment'></div>粗蒙一命之微，已致七年之废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206285_comment'></div>方睿主之有作，而公道之大行，乃于斯时，复与此选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206285_comment'></div>头童齿豁，敢辞乳媪之讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206285_comment'></div>闻浅见轻，但畏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1206285", 1206285, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>金根</span>之谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206285_comment'></div>顾惟忝冒，有愧情颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206285_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官乐育英材，修明前志，以冰鉴之平而邪正洞照，以湖海之量而细大毕收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206285_comment'></div>怜其衰残，借以光宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206285_comment'></div>老马伏枥，不忘万里之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206285_comment'></div>弱羽冲风，敢期百发之中！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206285_comment'></div>感幸之至，但切下情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1206285_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_155305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_155305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/155305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题王平甫帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34457, "北宋", "陈师道", "poem_title_155305")'>陈师道</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_155305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_155305'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_155305'>早闻英气擅家声，晚得诸郎识老成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_155305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_155305'>可恨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_155305", 155305, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>治朝</span>无此老，却嫌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_155305", 155305, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>晚进</span>不同生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_155305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_155305'>足知落笔千言疾，尚想挥毫一坐倾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_155305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_155305'>未信哲人穷五字，二难还复以诗鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_155305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_155305'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_155305_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
